Make a fresh clone of `chess-rtk` go from "I have Java" to "I ran a grounded analysis on my own game" in one guided command, on Linux today and Windows/macOS soon, without ever (a) shipping a false instruction, (b) running unverified downloaded binaries/weights, or (c) introducing a build dependency beyond `javac --release 17` + `jar` (CMake stays optional, for GPU only).

#### User story

> *A grad student clones the repo on Ubuntu and a colleague's MacBook. They run `crtk setup`. It checks Java 17, tells them Stockfish is missing and exactly how to get it for their OS, offers to download the default NNUE net (showing the size and SHA-256, verifying it after), drops a couple of sample PGNs in `examples/`, seeds `config/cli.config.toml`, and ends with three copy-pasteable commands. `crtk doctor` is green. Nothing they ran touched the network without telling them the URL and hash first.*

#### Non-goals

- **No** new build-system dependency. The `recommended`/`ci` targets in [run_regression_suite.sh](scripts/run_regression_suite.sh) must keep working with stock `javac` + `jar`; any packaging tooling (jpackage, fpm, scoop manifests) is *optional* and lives in `scripts/`, never on the compile path.
- **No** auto-installing system packages or GPU toolchains silently ŌĆö `crtk setup` *advises*; `install.sh` (which already does apt management) remains the privileged installer.
- **No** bundling model weights into git or the default release tarball (the `--include-models` flag on [make_release_linux_cuda.sh](scripts/make_release_linux_cuda.sh) stays opt-in; [check_no_weights_tracked.sh](scripts/check_no_weights_tracked.sh) keeps enforcing the gitignore policy).
- **No** telemetry, license servers, or phone-home. Provenance is local only.

---

#### MVP (smallest shippable)

Pure correctness + a thin onboarding command, no new platforms:

1. **Fix the false jar claim.** [wiki/getting-started.md:48](wiki/getting-started.md) says *"A prebuilt `crtk.jar` ships in the repository root."* It does not ŌĆö `crtk.jar` is gitignored ([.gitignore:31](.gitignore)). A clean clone has no jar and `java -jar crtk.jar version` fails. Either (a) change the doc to instruct `./scripts/run_regression_suite.sh jar` (or `build` then `java -cp out application.Main`) first, or (b) actually attach `crtk.jar` to GitHub Releases and point the doc at the release. (a) is the MVP; (b) belongs in tranche 3.
2. **Single-source the version.** `VERSION = "1.0.0"` is hard-coded in [VersionCommand.java:20](src/application/cli/command/VersionCommand.java) *and* `"version": "1.0.0"` in [package.json:3](package.json) with nothing enforcing agreement; [make_release_linux_cuda.sh](scripts/make_release_linux_cuda.sh) derives its own from `git describe`. Add a `SourceHeaderRegressionTest`-style check (or a new tiny `VersionConsistencyRegressionTest`) that asserts `VersionCommand.VERSION` equals the `package.json` version string. (Build-time injection from a git tag is nicer but is tranche 3.)
3. **Verify weight downloads.** [install.sh:22-27](install.sh) fetches the Stockfish NNUE, two LC0 CNNs, and BT4 via `download_file` ([install.sh:217](install.sh)) with **no checksum** ŌĆö unlike [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh) which already has `verify_sha256()` ([line 94](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh)) and a `--sha256` flag. MVP: add a parallel `MODEL_SHA256=( ŌĆ” )` array next to `MODEL_REMOTE_FILES` and call the existing verify path after each download; fail loud on mismatch. This is the same hash work I (provenance) needs, so do it once.
4. **Fix the classifier default-weights path drift.** `chess.nn.classifier.Model.DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` points at `models/classifier_21planes-ŌĆ”bin` but the file the install/README ship is `puzzle-classifier_21planes-ŌĆ”bin` ([models/README.md:29](models/README.md)), so `loadDefault()` fails out of the box. MVP: rename one to match the other (prefer making the constant match the shipped/README name) and add a regression that asserts `DEFAULT_WEIGHTS`'s filename appears in `models/README.md`.
5. **`crtk setup` (thin).** A new root leaf that orchestrates the checks already implemented in [DoctorCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/DoctorCommand.java) + [ConfigOps.java](src/application/cli/ConfigOps.java), seeds config if missing (reusing `Config.seedConfigIfMissing` at [Config.java:697](src/application/Config.java)), and prints next-step commands. MVP behavior = run the same validations doctor runs, plus per-OS Stockfish hints, plus "here are 3 commands to try." No interactivity required in MVP (a `--yes`-style non-interactive path is fine first).

#### Full version

- Interactive `crtk setup` wizard (prompts for: download default weights? install desktop entry? pick an external engine?) with a `--non-interactive`/`--yes` path for CI and a `--json` summary.
- `crtk engine detect` + install-hints across Linux/macOS/Windows.
- `crtk model list | download | verify` as a first-class, hash-checked weight manager that supersedes the two divergent fetch paths (`install.sh`'s table and `fetch_lc0_net.sh`).
- `crtk examples install` to drop curated sample PGNs/FENs/record dumps under `examples/`.
- `crtk doctor --fix-suggestions` (and `--json`) emitting actionable, copy-pasteable remediation per failed/warned check.
- Release artifacts beyond linux-cuda: a CPU-only portable tarball/zip (no native libs), plus `jpackage`-based self-contained bundles, and community-package manifests (`.deb` via fpm, Homebrew formula, Scoop/winget manifests).
- A real cross-platform launcher story so `crtk` works from anywhere, not just from the repo root.

---

#### Proposed CLI surface (noun-then-verb)

All new verbs route through [CliRegistry.buildRoot()](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) (today it registers `doctor`/`clean`/`version` as root leaves at lines 165/172/184 and a `config` group at line 768; there is **no** existing `setup`/`examples`/`detect`/`model` surface ŌĆö confirmed by grep). Exit codes follow the existing taxonomy: 0 ok, 1 strict-warning, 2 usage/error, 3 input-not-found.

```
### Onboarding orchestrator (root leaf, mirrors doctor's check engine)
crtk setup [--non-interactive|--yes] [--no-models] [--no-desktop] [--no-engine]
           [--json] [-v|--verbose]
    # runs the doctor checks, seeds config, prints OS-specific engine hints,
    # optionally invokes `model download` and `examples install`

### External-engine discovery (NO engine budgets here ŌĆö pure discovery)
crtk engine detect [--json]
    # probes PATH for stockfish/lc0 (PathOps.isExecutableOnPath), reports
    # version via a bounded `uci`+`quit` handshake, prints per-OS install hints
crtk engine install-hints [--os linux|macos|windows] [--engine stockfish|lc0]
    # prints the apt/brew/scoop/winget line; no execution

### Safe optional weights manager (replaces the two divergent fetch paths)
crtk model list [--json]                 # known models, expected SHA-256, local presence
crtk model download <name|all> [--dir models] [--no-verify] [--json]
                                         # downloads, then verifies SHA-256, fail-loud
crtk model verify [<name|all>] [--dir models] [--json]
                                         # checks on-disk files against expected hashes

### Sample content
crtk examples install [--dir examples] [--force] [--json]
crtk examples list [--json]

### Diagnostics upgrades (extend the existing leaf)
crtk doctor [--strict] [--fix-suggestions] [--json] [-v|--verbose]
crtk config show [--json]                # add --json (currently text-only)
crtk config validate                     # unchanged (already exits 1 warn / 2 error)
crtk version [--json|--jsonl]            # unchanged

### Where an engine is actually USED (existing commands, shown for budget grounding)
crtk engine uci-smoke -P config/default.engine.toml --nodes 1 --max-duration 5s
    # `crtk setup` ends by suggesting this exact bounded smoke test
```

Engine *budgets* (`--max-nodes`/`--max-duration`/`--threads`/`--hash`/`--multipv`) belong only on commands that actually search ŌĆö `engine detect` deliberately uses a 1-node/5s-style bounded handshake (mirroring the existing [uci-smoke](src/application/cli/command/UciSmokeCommand.java) default) and nothing heavier, so detection never hangs on a misbehaving engine.

#### Proposed Workbench surface (mirroring CLI, no second impl)

The Workbench already shells out to the real CLI via a child JVM ([CommandRunner.java:505](src/application/gui/workbench/command/CommandRunner.java) builds `java -cp <classpath> application.Main <args>`), so onboarding panels must invoke the same verbs, not reimplement them:

- **Dashboard "Setup" card / first-run banner-less prompt.** The design guide bans a hero banner, so this is a small status strip on the existing Dashboard ([DashboardPanel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/dashboard/DashboardPanel.java) via the [DashboardActions](src/application/gui/workbench/dashboard/DashboardActions.java) interface): "Java 17 ok ┬Ę Stockfish missing ┬Ę Default net not downloaded" with buttons that run `crtk engine detect`, `crtk model download`, `crtk examples install` through `CommandRunner`. The "Run all health checks" action already exists (`runAllHealthChecks`) ŌĆö extend it to surface `doctor --fix-suggestions`.
- **Model manager view** is a thin table over `crtk model list --json` with a Download button per row that runs `crtk model download <name>` and shows the verify result. No download logic in Swing; it parses JSON the CLI prints.
- The generated command preview must equal the runnable command (enforced by [WorkbenchCommandRegression.testCommandControllerCoversCliRegistry](src/testing/WorkbenchCommandRegression.java)), so any new leaf is auto-covered by that test the moment it lands in the registry.

---

#### Data model / schema implications (concrete fields)

1. **A model catalog** ŌĆö the single source of truth that replaces the parallel arrays in [install.sh:22-30](install.sh) and the ad-hoc URL in [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh). Ship it as a tracked TOML (consistent with `config/*.toml` and parsed by the existing dependency-free `utility.Toml`), e.g. `config/models.toml`:
   ```toml
   [[model]]
   name        = "nnue-default"
   kind        = "nnue"                 # nnue|lc0-cnn|bt4|otis|classifier|t5
   local_file  = "crtk-halfkp.nnue"     # resolved under models/
   url         = "https://tests.stockfishchess.org/api/nn/nn-fcf986aea78a.nnue"
   sha256      = "<hex>"
   bytes       = 0
   license     = "GPL-3.0-only"         # upstream net terms
   default_for = ["engine builtin --nnue"]
   optional    = true
   ```
   `crtk model list/download/verify` and `install.sh` both read this; the install script's bash can `python3`-or-`grep` it, but the canonical reader is a small `chess.io`/`application` loader so the CLI is authoritative.
2. **`crtk version --json`** keeps its shape `{name, launcher, version, java}` ([VersionCommand.java:56-59](src/application/cli/command/VersionCommand.java)); add an optional `commit` field once build-time injection lands (tranche 3).
3. **`crtk doctor --json`** ŌĆö a new stable object (depends on F's schema work), e.g.
   ```json
   {"schema":"crtk.doctor.v1","status":"ok-with-warnings","java":"17.0.x",
    "config":"ŌĆ”","protocol":"ŌĆ”","engineInstances":4,"output":"dump/",
    "checks":[{"id":"java","ok":true},{"id":"stockfish-on-path","ok":false,
      "fix":"sudo apt-get install stockfish"}],
    "warnings":[ŌĆ”],"errors":[ŌĆ”]}
   ```
   The status strings already exist as plain text (`ok`/`ok-with-warnings`/`failed`/`failed-strict`, [DoctorCommand.java:122-127](src/application/cli/command/DoctorCommand.java)); `--json` just serializes them plus a `fix` per check.

No change to the `.record` / dataset schemas here ŌĆö but the SHA-256 model hashes produced for this initiative are exactly what I (provenance) stamps into export `meta.json`, so define them once.

---

#### Architecture implications

- **Plain build is sacrosanct.** Everything above compiles with `javac --release 17`. The model catalog parser reuses the existing in-house `utility.Toml` (already used for `config/*.toml` and the ECO book), so no new dep. JSON output reuses `utility.Json` / `CommandSupport.jsonString` (as `VersionCommand` already does).
- **No new HTTP client in Java.** `crtk model download` shells to `curl`/`wget` (the same tools [install.sh:224-229](install.sh) already requires) via `ProcessBuilder`, then verifies with Java's `MessageDigest` (JDK built-in, no dep). This keeps the Java side dependency-free and avoids embedding a downloader. The bash `install.sh` path and the Java `crtk model` path call the *same* catalog and *same* verify logic conceptually; long-term, `install.sh` can simply invoke `java -cp out application.Main model download all` after the build step, collapsing the two implementations.
- **Optional deps stay isolated.** GPU toolchains (CUDA/ROCm/oneAPI via CMake) remain entirely inside `install.sh`'s backend-build functions and `native/*/`; `crtk setup` only *reports* their presence (mirroring `crtk engine gpu`), never builds them.
- **Relative-path footgun.** Config/models resolve against CWD ([Config.java](src/application/Config.java) uses relative defaults; `configuration.md` warns about this), so `crtk` only "just works" from the repo root unless launched via the generated launcher that `cd`s to `APP_HOME` ([install.sh:13](install.sh)). The cross-platform launchers (tranche 3) must replicate that `cd $APP_HOME` behavior; `crtk doctor` should warn when CWD ŌēĀ resolved config dir and the config/model files are not found.

---

#### Existing components to reuse (real files)

- [install.sh](install.sh) ŌĆö prereq checks, apt management, model fetch table, native backend builds, launcher + `crtk-workbench.desktop` generation. `crtk setup` advises; `install.sh` executes privileged steps.
- [scripts/update.sh](scripts/update.sh), [scripts/uninstall.sh](scripts/uninstall.sh) ŌĆö ff-only update and repo-scoped removal; the cross-platform story must preserve their guardrails.
- [scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh) ŌĆö the existing `verify_sha256()` + `--sha256` path; converge `crtk model` and `install.sh` onto it.
- [scripts/make_release_linux_cuda.sh](scripts/make_release_linux_cuda.sh) ŌĆö the only release packager (stages `crtk.jar`, `lib/liblc0_cuda.so`, launcher, LICENSE, README, config/, wiki/, writes `dist/SHA256SUMS`); template for a CPU-only and other-OS bundles.
- [DoctorCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/DoctorCommand.java) + [ConfigOps.java](src/application/cli/ConfigOps.java) ŌĆö the check engine (`validateProtocolConfig`, `validateProtocolFile`, `PathOps.isExecutableOnPath` at [ConfigOps.java:106](src/application/cli/ConfigOps.java)); `setup`, `engine detect`, and `doctor --fix-suggestions` all build on these.
- [PathOps.isExecutableOnPath](src/application/cli/PathOps.java) ([line 39](src/application/cli/PathOps.java), splits `$PATH` on `File.pathSeparator`) ŌĆö already cross-platform-aware; `engine detect` reuses it directly.
- [Config.java](src/application/Config.java) ŌĆö `seedConfigIfMissing` ([line 697](src/application/Config.java)), `getConfigPath` ([623](src/application/Config.java)), `publishRuntimeDefaults` ([810](src/application/Config.java)).
- [VersionCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/VersionCommand.java), [CleanCommand](src/application/cli/command/CleanCommand.java), [ConfigCommand](src/application/cli/command/ConfigCommand.java) ŌĆö existing onboarding/diagnostic leaves to sit beside.
- [models/README.md](models/README.md) ŌĆö the self-describing filename convention and the tracked-weights policy `crtk model` must honor.
- [InstallScriptRegressionTest.java](src/testing/InstallScriptRegressionTest.java) ŌĆö pattern for asserting launcher shell-quoting and desktop-entry icon; extend for new launcher variants.

#### Files / packages likely affected

- New: `src/application/cli/command/SetupCommand.java`, `EngineDetectCommand.java`, `ModelCommand.java`, `ExamplesCommand.java`; a `config/models.toml`; an `examples/` directory of sample PGN/FEN/`.record`.
- Modified: [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) (register `setup`, `engine detect`/`install-hints`, `model ŌĆ”`, `examples ŌĆ”`; add `--fix-suggestions`/`--json` to `doctor`, `--json` to `config show`), [DoctorCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/DoctorCommand.java) (JSON + fix suggestions + Stockfish-on-PATH check), [ConfigOps.java](src/application/cli/ConfigOps.java) (shared catalog/engine probes), [VersionCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/VersionCommand.java) (single-source consistency), [install.sh](install.sh) (per-model SHA-256, optionally delegate to `crtk model`), [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh) (point at `config/models.toml`), [models/README.md](models/README.md) + [getting-started.md](wiki/getting-started.md) (fix the jar claim), [chess/nn/classifier/Model.java](src/chess/nn/classifier/Model.java) (`DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` filename fix).
- New scripts (tranche 3, optional, not on compile path): `scripts/make_release_portable.sh` (CPU-only tarball/zip), `scripts/package_deb.sh` (fpm), `packaging/homebrew/crtk.rb`, `packaging/scoop/crtk.json`, `packaging/winget/`, plus `crtk.cmd`/`crtk.ps1` launchers.

---

#### Testing plan (in-house harness style ŌĆö `public static void main`, `testing.TestSupport.*`)

- **`VersionConsistencyRegressionTest`** ŌĆö reads `package.json` and asserts its `"version"` equals `VersionCommand.VERSION`; asserts `make_release_linux_cuda.sh` default-version logic doesn't contradict (string-presence check).
- **`ModelCatalogRegressionTest`** ŌĆö parses `config/models.toml`; asserts every `local_file` matches the [models/README.md](models/README.md) naming table and that `chess.nn.classifier.Model.DEFAULT_WEIGHTS`, `chess.nn.otis.Model.DEFAULT_WEIGHTS`, and the default `lc0-model-path` all appear as catalog entries (catches the classifier path drift permanently).
- **`ModelVerifyRegressionTest`** ŌĆö writes a tiny temp file with a known SHA-256, runs `crtk model verify` against a catalog pointing at it via `TestSupport.runMain` / `runMainExpectFailure`, asserts exit 0 on match and exit 3 (or 2) on mismatch; asserts a corrupted byte fails loud.
- **`DoctorJsonRegressionTest`** ŌĆö `runMain("doctor","--json")`, parse with `utility.Json`, assert `schema`/`status`/`checks[]` present and that `status` Ōłł {ok, ok-with-warnings, failed, failed-strict}; assert `doctor --strict` returns exit 1 when only warnings (matching [status()](src/application/cli/command/DoctorCommand.java)).
- **`SetupCommandRegressionTest`** ŌĆö `runMain("setup","--non-interactive","--no-models","--no-desktop")` from a temp CWD with no config; assert it seeds config (`Config.getConfigPath` now exists), prints the three suggested commands, and exits 0; assert `--no-models` performs no network calls (inject a catalog with an unreachable URL and assert it is *not* contacted).
- **`EngineDetectRegressionTest`** ŌĆö reuse the [UCIRegressionTest](src/testing/UCIRegressionTest.java) `fake-uci.sh` shell engine on PATH; assert `engine detect --json` reports it found, with a version line, using a bounded handshake (no long search); skip the live-Stockfish leg unless `CRTK_REQUIRE_STOCKFISH=1` (mirroring the existing convention).
- **`ExamplesInstallRegressionTest`** ŌĆö `runMain("examples","install","--dir",<temp>)`; assert the sample files appear and that re-running without `--force` does not clobber edits.
- **Extend [InstallScriptRegressionTest](src/testing/InstallScriptRegressionTest.java)** ŌĆö assert `install.sh` now defines a per-model SHA-256 array and calls a verify step after `download_file`; assert any new `crtk.ps1`/`crtk.cmd` launchers `cd` to `APP_HOME` before launching (the relative-path footgun).
- **Wire into the runner.** Add the above to the `cli`/`core` targets in [run_regression_suite.sh](scripts/run_regression_suite.sh) so they actually gate CI (the digest flagged six existing tests that are *not* wired in ŌĆö do not repeat that mistake here).

#### Docs plan

- [wiki/getting-started.md](wiki/getting-started.md) ŌĆö fix the false `crtk.jar`-ships claim; lead with `crtk setup`.
- [wiki/build-and-install.md](wiki/build-and-install.md) (referenced from getting-started:55) ŌĆö document `crtk setup`, `engine detect`, `model list/download/verify`, `examples install`, and the per-OS matrix.
- [wiki/configuration.md](wiki/configuration.md) ŌĆö document `config/models.toml` and the CWD/relative-path resolution rule plus the doctor warning.
- [wiki/troubleshooting.md](wiki/troubleshooting.md) + [wiki/support.md](wiki/support.md) ŌĆö point users at `doctor --fix-suggestions`.
- [wiki/releasing.md](wiki/releasing.md) ŌĆö record the single-source version rule (it already warns the tag/jar/version mismatch is "the bug nobody notices") and the new release artifacts.
- [models/README.md](models/README.md) ŌĆö note `crtk model` as the canonical fetcher; keep the naming convention as the catalog's contract.

---

#### Risks / tradeoffs

- **Two download paths drifting.** `install.sh` (bash) and `crtk model` (Java) can diverge again. Mitigation: one tracked `config/models.toml` both read; long-term, `install.sh` delegates to `crtk model download` after build.
- **Hash maintenance burden.** Pinning SHA-256 means upstream net updates require a catalog edit. Acceptable ŌĆö that is the point of reproducibility; `crtk model verify` makes drift visible rather than silent.
- **`crtk setup` scope creep toward an installer.** Keep the privilege boundary: `setup` never `sudo`s or installs system packages; it advises and downloads user-space artifacts only. `install.sh` stays the privileged path.
- **Cross-platform launcher correctness.** The Linux launcher's `cd $APP_HOME` + `-Djava.library.path` assembly ([install.sh:1166+](install.sh)) is non-trivial; naive `.cmd`/`.ps1` ports will hit the relative-path footgun. Mitigation: regression-test the `cd`-to-APP_HOME behavior; ship CPU-only bundles first (no native libs ŌćÆ no `java.library.path` complexity).
- **`jpackage`/fpm add hidden toolchain needs** (WiX on Windows, `dpkg`/`fpm` on Linux). Keep them strictly in `scripts/`, invoked manually for releases, never in `ci`/`recommended`.
- **License propagation.** Bundled upstream nets carry their own terms (README already notes this); the catalog's `license` field and a per-artifact license note in releases reduce the risk. No SBOM today ŌĆö flagged as future.

---

#### Acceptance criteria (checkable)

1. A clean clone + `./scripts/run_regression_suite.sh build` (no manual jar step) lets `java -cp out application.Main version` run, and [getting-started.md](wiki/getting-started.md) contains no instruction that fails on a clean clone (grep test).
2. `VersionCommand.VERSION` == `package.json` version, enforced by a wired-in regression.
3. `install.sh` verifies every fetched weight's SHA-256 and aborts on mismatch; `crtk model verify all` exits 0 on a correct `models/` tree and non-zero with a named file on corruption.
4. `chess.nn.classifier.Model.loadDefault()` succeeds against the file `install.sh`/README ship (filename drift gone, asserted by `ModelCatalogRegressionTest`).
5. `crtk setup --non-interactive` from an empty CWD seeds config, prints OS-correct Stockfish hints, and exits 0 without any network access when `--no-models` is given.
6. `crtk engine detect --json` finds a Stockfish-on-PATH (or the fake-uci test engine) and reports a version via a bounded handshake.
7. `crtk doctor --json` emits a `crtk.doctor.v1` object whose `status` matches the text mode, and `--fix-suggestions` prints a remediation line per failed check.
8. All new commands appear in `crtk help`, are covered by `WorkbenchCommandRegression`, and the new tests are listed in the `cli`/`core` targets of [run_regression_suite.sh](scripts/run_regression_suite.sh).

---

#### Future expansion

- **Build-time version injection** from `git describe` into a generated `Version` constant (removes the duplication entirely; needs a codegen step kept off the simple path ŌĆö emit a `.java` during `build`).
- **CPU-only portable bundle** (`scripts/make_release_portable.sh`): `crtk.jar` + launchers for all three OSes, no native libs ŌĆö the lowest-risk cross-platform artifact, ship first.
- **`jpackage` self-contained apps** (bundled JRE) for the Workbench, per-OS, behind a release-only script.
- **Community manifests**: `.deb` (fpm), Homebrew formula, Scoop bucket, winget manifest ŌĆö each just fetches the portable bundle and drops a launcher; sequence after the portable bundle exists.
- **SBOM + per-artifact license file** in releases (upstream net terms, GPL-3.0-only core).
- **`crtk setup` deep links into I/C**: once a PGN store (A) and review router (C) exist, `examples install` seeds a sample game and `setup` can end with "now run `crtk pgn import examples/sample.pgn` and `crtk ŌĆ” review`."

---

#### Sequencing summary

| Tranche | Items | Term | Priority | Complexity |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 ŌĆö correctness | jar doc-drift, version single-source, weight SHA-256, classifier path | short-term | **P0ŌĆōP1** | small |
| 2 ŌĆö onboarding | `crtk setup`, `engine detect`/`install-hints`, `model list/download/verify`, `examples install`, `doctor --fix-suggestions`/`--json`, `config show --json` | medium-term | **P2** | medium |
| 3 ŌĆö distribution | CPU-only + jpackage bundles, `.deb`/Homebrew/Scoop/winget, cross-platform launchers, build-time version injection | long-term | **P2ŌĆōP3** | largeŌåÆxlarge |

**Cross-platform reality:** packaging is currently 100% Linux/Debian-Ubuntu-apt ([install.sh:5](install.sh) is explicitly Ubuntu-scoped; the only release packager is linux-cuda; the launcher targets `/usr/local/bin` + freedesktop `.desktop`). Java itself is portable ŌĆö *only the packaging is not*. The safe path that does not break the simple build: keep `javac --release 17` + the portable jar as the universal baseline, ship a CPU-only cross-platform bundle next, and add OS-specific package managers last, each as an optional `scripts/`/`packaging/` artifact that fetches the already-built jar rather than recompiling.

---


## 9. Suggested new command areas

The CLI today has 10 noun groups ŌĆö `record`, `fen`, `gen`, `batch`, `move`, `engine`, `position`, `book`, `puzzle`, `config` ŌĆö plus root leaves `mate`, `gauntlet`, `workbench`, `doctor`, `clean`, `help`, `version` (verified in [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) `buildRoot()`). The grammar is noun-then-verb. This section evaluates 12 candidate new areas against that grammar and the hard product boundary (no online play / matchmaking / social / anti-cheat / cloud, no chasing Stockfish strength; reference-grade analysis goes through external UCI). Each verdict is decisive.

A recurring structural point: several proposed areas are really **promotions of existing in-process or workbench-only logic into the shared core + a CLI peer**, not greenfield work. That is the cheap, high-leverage path and is called out where it applies.

---

### `db` ŌĆö local game/record store ŌĆö **DEFER ŌåÆ fold into `game`**

**Verdict: NO as a standalone area; its job is the storage layer under `game`.** A separate `db` area implies an indexed, queryable on-disk store. That capability is needed, but exposing it as its own noun fragments the user's mental model: a student thinks "my games", not "my database". The store is an implementation detail of `game` (and a consumer of the schema work). Today there is **no** persistent store at all ŌĆö [PgnExplorerModel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) indexes and filters games purely in-memory and workbench-only, with no CLI peer, no game-id, no on-disk index (the digest and a registry grep both confirm only stateless `fen pgn` / `record export pgn` / `puzzle pgn` exist). Build the store, but surface it through `game` verbs, not a `db` noun. The one defensible reason to keep `db` separate would be raw index maintenance (`db reindex`, `db compact`), which can live as `game reindex` instead.

**Difficulty if pursued separately: large** (and redundant with `game`).

---

### `import` ŌĆö bring games/positions in ŌĆö **DEFER ŌåÆ fold into `game import`**

**Verdict: NO as a standalone area; it is one verb of `game`.** Importing is an action on the game store, not its own object. A top-level `import` noun has no other verbs that make sense (`import import`?). The legitimate scope ŌĆö read-only ingestion of a local PGN/EPD/`.record` file or directory into the store ŌĆö belongs as `game import`. **Boundary caution that makes this DEFER rather than YES:** any networked import (lichess/chess.com fetch) sits closest to the forbidden online/social space and must be strictly read-only, on-demand, file-or-public-export only ŌĆö and even then it is low value over "export your games and import the PGN". Local-file import folds into `game`; networked import is a P3 decision deferred until `game` exists. Reuses [Pgn.java](src/chess/struct/Pgn.java) and [Reader.java](src/chess/io/Reader.java).

**Difficulty (local-file import as part of `game`): small-to-medium.**

---

### `game` ŌĆö local PGN database / ChessBase-lite ŌĆö **YES (P1)**

**Verdict: YES.** This is the single biggest missing product foundation and it is squarely in-boundary (local files, not online play). The substrate exists but is inert: [Game.java](src/chess/struct/Game.java)/[Pgn.java](src/chess/struct/Pgn.java) parse and round-trip with a variation tree, [Reader.java](src/chess/io/Reader.java)/[Writer.java](src/chess/io/Writer.java)/[Converter.java](src/chess/io/Converter.java) merge and link records, and the workbench already has [PgnExplorerModel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) (index/filter/dedupe) and [PgnPrepReport.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnPrepReport.java) ŌĆö but all are in-memory, GUI-only, with no game-id, no provenance, and no on-disk index. The plan: promote `PgnExplorerModel`'s index/filter logic into `chess.*` core (so CLI and workbench share one implementation, preserving the one-shared-core and CLI-is-source-of-truth values), back it with a JSONL/`.record` store keyed on a game-id plus [Position.signatureCore()](src/chess/core/Position.java) position index. Depends on the schema area landing first (the store needs a versioned on-disk format and the game-id/provenance fields [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) currently lacks).

**Example commands**
- `crtk game import --input games.pgn` (also accepts a directory; folds in `import`)
- `crtk game query --white "Carlsen" --eco "B90" --result "1-0"`
- `crtk game show --id <game-id> --format pgn`
- `crtk game stats --input store/`

**Artifacts:** an on-disk store directory (JSONL/`.record` shards + a position-signature index file); query results as JSON/JSONL/PGN on stdout; per-game provenance (source file checksum, import time, game-id).

**Difficulty: large.**

---

### `study` ŌĆö game-review-to-study router ŌĆö **YES (P1, after `game` + `schema`)**

**Verdict: YES, but sequenced.** All grounded primitives exist and none of them are wired into a router. `fen tags --pgn <file> --analyze-game` (verified in [TagsCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/TagsCommand.java), `--analyze-game` requires `--pgn`) already emits whole-game MOVE/LINE/VARIATION/GAME annotation via [GameAnalyzer.java](src/chess/tag/game/GameAnalyzer.java) and [LineAnalyzer.java](src/chess/tag/game/LineAnalyzer.java); [RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java) summarizes eval drift; the miner ([MineCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/MineCommand.java)) turns a FEN into a puzzle. What is missing across the whole repo is the verb that ingests a played game, detects the blunder/turning-point, and emits study units ŌĆö the "the human played X, the puzzle is the refutation" pipeline the miner explicitly does *not* do. **Honest blocker:** the engine-graded `quality=`/`turning_point` MOVE_EFFECT verdicts are deferred/TODO (per the tag digest); until they land, grading must route through external UCI ([Engine.java](src/chess/uci/Engine.java) + [Pool.java](src/application/Pool.java)). Depends on `game` (input) and `schema` (a stable study-unit output contract).

**Example commands**
- `crtk study review --input mygame.pgn --engine-protocol config/default.engine.toml`
- `crtk study extract --input mygame.pgn --threshold-cp 150` (emit puzzle records for each detected mistake's refutation)
- `crtk study annotate --id <game-id> --output annotated.pgn`

**Artifacts:** study-unit `.record`/JSONL (one row per detected mistake, carrying the refutation line + grounded tags); annotated PGN with NAGs.

**Difficulty: large.**

---

### `explain` ŌĆö grounded natural-language explanation ŌĆö **DEFER ŌåÆ keep under existing nouns**

**Verdict: NO as a new area; the capability is already PRESENT and correctly placed.** The grounded-explanation layer is the project's core preserved value and already exists as `position describe` ([ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java), faithful-by-construction, with opt-in [EngineEvaluator.java](src/chess/describe/EngineEvaluator.java) that corrects false static verdicts), `fen text` / `puzzle text` ([Runner.java](src/chess/nn/t5/Runner.java)), and `fen relations` (visual OTIS grounding). Adding an `explain` noun would duplicate verbs that already live sensibly on `position`, `fen`, and `puzzle`. The work this theme needs is **deepening** (turning the already-collected-but-unused KingSafety/Structure/passers tags into "why/plan" sentences; audience tuning) and **honesty hardening** ŌĆö the generative T5 path ships no weights ([T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java) `available()` is permanently `false`) and the documented inference-time grounding/verification pass (legal-SAN check, fallback-to-classical) is unimplemented. That is improvement to existing commands, not a new area. Sequence after `study` so explanations have whole-game context.

**Difficulty (deepening existing commands): medium.**

---

### `schema` ŌĆö machine-readable command catalog + JSON Schema artifacts ŌĆö **YES (P0)**

**Verdict: YES, highest priority, lowest cost.** This is the precondition for `game`, `study`, `dataset` provenance, `serve`, and editor tooling ŌĆö nothing can build a stable contract on prose help tables. Verified gaps: there are **zero** `*.schema.json` files in the repo; there is no `crtk help --json` / `crtk schema` command even though [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) already holds every path, flag, example, and exit code in memory; [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) has **no** schema-version field; and `Record.fromJson` / [Reader.java](src/chess/io/Reader.java) silently drop malformed input. Concrete scope: (1) serialize the registry to a catalog command; (2) add `schemaVersion` to `Record` and publish JSON Schema files for `.record`, `training-jsonl`, dataset `meta.json`, and the per-command JSON shapes; (3) a strict validate path that fails loudly. The existing [RunManifest.java](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java) (`crtk.workbench.run-manifest.v1` + per-file SHA-256) is the pattern to mirror. Reuses canonical metadata rather than inventing it.

**Example commands**
- `crtk schema commands` (emit the full area/action/flag/exit-code catalog as JSON)
- `crtk schema show record` (emit the JSON Schema for a `.record` file)
- `crtk schema validate --input data.record` (fail-loud, report malformed rows instead of dropping them)

**Artifacts:** a JSON command catalog; published `*.schema.json` files under a `schema/` dir; non-zero exit on contract violation.

**Difficulty: medium.**

---

### `dataset` ŌĆö ML dataset export/provenance ŌĆö **DEFER ŌåÆ keep under `record`, fix provenance in place**

**Verdict: NO as a new top-level area; partially exists already and should stay under `record`.** Datasets are export *views of records*, so `record dataset {npy,lc0,classifier}` and `record export {training-jsonl,puzzle-jsonl,puzzle-elo-jsonl}` are correctly placed today (verified in [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) lines 262ŌĆō276 and 246ŌĆō256). Promoting `dataset` to a top-level noun would orphan it from the records it derives from. The real work is **fixing the overstated provenance promise in place** (P1, medium): `record dataset npy` writes **no** `meta.json` at all (confirmed in [RecordDatasetExporter.java](src/chess/io/RecordDatasetExporter.java) ŌĆö only `.features.npy`/`.labels.npy`), no exporter records crtk version / git commit / input checksums / weights hash, and [Model.java](src/chess/nn/classifier/Model.java) `DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` points at `classifier_ŌĆ”` while the shipped file is `puzzle-classifier_ŌĆ”` (a broken `loadDefault()`). Add a uniform provenance stamp to every exporter (reusing the [RunManifest.java](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java) SHA-256 pattern), converge weight fetching on the sha256-verifying path in [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh), and fix the classifier path. This pairs with `schema`.

**Example commands (existing, to be hardened ŌĆö not new):** `crtk record dataset npy ŌĆ”`, `crtk record dataset lc0 ŌĆ”`, `crtk record export training-jsonl ŌĆ”`.

**Difficulty (provenance hardening, no new area): medium.**

---

### `serve` ŌĆö localhost analysis/automation daemon + SDK seam ŌĆö **DEFER (P2, after `schema`)**

**Verdict: NO now; revisit after `schema`.** Verified absent (no `ServerSocket`/`HttpServer`/`com.sun.net.httpserver` in `src`). The in-process engine APIs ([AlphaBeta.java](src/chess/engine/AlphaBeta.java), [Mcts.java](src/chess/engine/Mcts.java), `MateProver`, `See`) and the minimal UCI loops are a genuine SDK seam, and every CLI invocation today pays JVM-startup latency, so a daemon has real value for interactive agents and editor tooling. But it is premature: a server built before `schema` would hard-code the very contracts `schema` is meant to standardize, guaranteeing drift. **Boundary caution:** acceptable ONLY as a localhost analysis/automation daemon ŌĆö it must never drift toward online play/matchmaking/cloud-credit. Once `schema` exists, a thin localhost JSON-RPC over [Main.java](src/application/Main.java) plus generated SDK stubs is far cheaper and stays in sync. The streaming hook already exists ([Engine.java](src/chess/uci/Engine.java) `analyseInfinite`/`onUpdate`).

**Difficulty: large.**

---

### `model` ŌĆö neural-net management (list/verify/train) ŌĆö **DEFER (P2, narrow scope only)**

**Verdict: NO for training; DEFER a narrow `list/verify` slice.** There is **no** training CLI today (a grep finds only a "future model training" comment in [PositionDescribeCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/PositionDescribeCommand.java); training lives in the external chess-nn-playground repo) and bringing trainers in-process fights the plain-`javac`/no-deps build and the deterministic-output value. A *management* slice is defensible but low-priority: weights are fetched ad hoc by [install.sh](install.sh) with **no** checksum verification (unlike [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh)), there is no manifest, and the classifier default path is broken. A small `model list` / `model verify` (checksum + magic-header check against [Model.java](src/chess/nn/otis/Model.java) loaders) would harden the supply chain ŌĆö but most of that value is captured by the `dataset`/`schema` provenance fixes plus fixing the classifier path. Training is rejected as out-of-boundary for the build constraints; management is deferred behind higher-leverage work.

**Example commands (narrow slice, if pursued):**
- `crtk model list` (enumerate `models/*.bin` with backend + parameter count)
- `crtk model verify --weights models/foo.bin --sha256 <hash>`

**Artifacts:** a model manifest with checksums and shapes.

**Difficulty (management slice): small. Training: xlarge and out of boundary ŌĆö rejected.**

---

### `plugin` ŌĆö third-party extension hooks ŌĆö **NO (reject)**

**Verdict: REJECT.** Explicitly a non-goal in-repo ([TODO.txt](TODO.txt) states "NON-GOAL: a plugin framework or a parallel docking system"). The command tree is a static singleton ([CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) `buildRoot()`), evaluators are a closed enum, and backends are hand-enumerated by design. A plugin system directly undermines the core preserved values: it puts third-party code in the deterministic pipeline (breaking reproducible outputs), conflicts with the no-third-party-deps / plain-`javac` build, and adds large maintenance and security surface for a single-maintainer project. The one legitimate extension need ŌĆö adding a UCI engine ŌĆö is *already* met by config-as-extension: a new engine is a [Protocol.java](src/chess/uci/Protocol.java) TOML, not code. Keep that seam healthy; do not build a plugin loader.

**Difficulty: large (and rejected on principle, not cost).**

---

### `otb` ŌĆö over-the-board / broadcast ingestion ŌĆö **NO (reject)**

**Verdict: REJECT.** Verified absent everywhere. OTB/broadcast (DGT boards, live relay, tournament feeds) pulls hard toward the live/online space the product boundary forbids, and even the "analyze a relayed game" slice requires real-time device/serial/network I/O and stateful streaming that contradicts the deterministic, process-per-invocation, local-artifact architecture. It serves tournament organizers/broadcasters ŌĆö an audience orthogonal to the study/research/ML/publishing users CRTK targets. The in-boundary answer for a relayed game already exists: export its PGN and use `game`/`study`. Premature and misaligned; reject.

**Difficulty: xlarge.**

---

### `scan` ŌĆö OCR diagram/scoresheet to study ŌĆö **NO (reject)**

**Verdict: REJECT.** Verified absent (the book pipeline is strictly authorŌåÆPDF; input is FEN/tags only). A real OCR pipeline (board-imageŌåÆFEN, scoresheetŌåÆPGN) needs a computer-vision model and training data that do not exist in-repo and cannot be produced under the no-third-party-deps / plain-`javac` constraint without a heavy native dependency or a bundled model the project has no pipeline to build ŌĆö both at odds with the no-deps and reproducibility values. It is a self-contained research project, not an increment on the toolkit. If ever pursued, it belongs in the external chess-nn-playground as a separate recognizer whose FEN/PGN output CRTK consumes via `game import` ŌĆö i.e. it reduces to "import a PGN" once an external tool does the recognition. Reject for now.

**Difficulty: xlarge.**

---

### Summary

| Area | Verdict | Priority | Difficulty | Already partial? |
|------|---------|----------|------------|------------------|
| `schema` | **YES** | P0 | medium | catalog metadata exists in `CliRegistry`, not serialized |
| `game` | **YES** | P1 | large | in-memory/workbench-only (`PgnExplorerModel`) |
| `study` | **YES** | P1 | large | primitives exist (`fen tags --analyze-game`, miner) |
| `db` | NO ŌåÆ fold into `game` | ŌĆö | large | none |
| `import` | NO ŌåÆ fold into `game import` | ŌĆö | smallŌĆōmed | stateless `fen pgn` only |
| `explain` | NO ŌåÆ deepen `position describe` | P1 | medium | PRESENT (`position describe`, `fen text`) |
| `dataset` | NO ŌåÆ keep under `record`, fix provenance | P1 | medium | PRESENT (`record dataset/export`) |
| `serve` | DEFER | P2 | large | absent (engine APIs are a seam) |
| `model` | DEFER (mgmt only) | P2 | small / xlarge | absent; training out of boundary |
| `plugin` | **REJECT** | ŌĆö | large | in-repo non-goal |
| `otb` | **REJECT** | ŌĆö | xlarge | absent, out of boundary |
| `scan` | **REJECT** | ŌĆö | xlarge | absent, out of boundary |

The decisive ordering: `schema` (P0) unblocks everything; `game` and `study` (P1) are the actual study-mission foundations; `explain` and `dataset` are P1 *improvements to existing commands*, not new nouns; `serve`/`model` defer behind `schema`; `plugin`/`otb`/`scan` are rejected as boundary violations or premature research projects.

---

## 10. Workbench redesign / productization

The full Workbench redesign/productization deep-dive lives in **[Section 8H](#8h-workbench-productization-and-section-10-redesign-detail)** (theme H: P2, build-later ŌĆö *deepen, do not expand*). This section surfaces the persona, first-run, and example-workflow specifics from 8H so the productization story reads as one piece; it does not duplicate 8H's testing plan, file list, or acceptance criteria ŌĆö consult 8H for those.

The single governing judgment (from 8H): the Workbench is already the most-developed surface in the repo (a shipped registry-driven 8-view shell ŌĆö [WindowLifecycle.java](src/application/gui/workbench/window/WindowLifecycle.java):1026-1056), so the redesign is **reorganization, persona framing, and CLI-mirror hardening ŌĆö not a UI rewrite**. It must remain a thin mirror of the CLI ([CommandRunner.java](src/application/gui/workbench/command/CommandRunner.java):505-511 spawns the real `application.Main` in a child JVM) and must consume the new A/C/F capabilities rather than fork them.

### 10.1 Persona presets (the core productization move)

Personas are **presets that pre-select a surface, a board/engine mode, an inspector layout, and a curated command-template subset** ŌĆö implemented as data over the existing `ViewRegistry`/`SwitchedWorkspace`, never as new code paths or hidden behavior. A `Persona` enum + a `PersonaPreset` record (`{landingView, boardMode, engineMode, templateNames, inspectorSections}`) drives emphasis only; *every persona can still reach every runnable command* (a machine-checked invariant ŌĆö see 8H test #2).

| Persona | Lands on | Mode | Curated focus | Maps to existing |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Beginner Review** | Board ŌåÆ Review | Analyze | `engine analyze`, `position describe`; explanations foregrounded, budgets hidden behind "Advanced" | `GameReviewPanel`, `PositionDescriptionPanel` |
| **Club Study** | Board ŌåÆ Study/ECO | Analyze + Solve | `fen tags`, `puzzle tags`, study author; opening tree visible | `StudyAuthorPanel`, `EcoExplorerPanel`, `PuzzlePanel` |
| **Coach** | Board ŌåÆ Review + Publish | Analyze | review ŌåÆ annotate ŌåÆ `book study`/`book pdf`; publish preview adjacent | `GameReviewPanel` + Publish surface |
| **Research / ML** | Datasets | ŌĆö | `record dataset {npy,lc0,classifier}`, `record export *-jsonl`, batch; budgets always visible | Datasets surface, batch templates |
| **Engine Lab** | Engine Lab | ŌĆö | `engine search`/`tree`/`trace`/`gauntlet --sprt`/`gpu` | Engine Lab modes |
| **Publishing** | Publish | ŌĆö | `book collection/render/cover/study/pdf` with `--check` dry-run | Publish surface |
| **Developer** | Run ŌåÆ Build | ŌĆö | "All CLI" template, batch run, console/logs, `doctor`, `config validate` | Run surface, Console, Logs |

Persona choice persists via the existing `WORKBENCH_PREFS` Preferences node; it changes which views/templates are emphasized, never which commands are runnable.

### 10.2 First-run flow

First launch has no persisted persona. The Dashboard renders its normal calm grid **plus** a single dismissible "Pick your workflow" card with the 7 persona chips ŌĆö *no hero banner, no modal* (the design guide bans both, [workbench-design-guide.md](wiki/workbench-design-guide.md):119). Selecting a persona records it, switches to that persona's landing surface, removes the card, and replaces it with a quiet status-strip hint ("Press ŌīśK for commands ┬Ę all results show their `crtk` command"). `crtk doctor`/`config validate` run silently on first launch and surface a single amber chip if the environment is unhealthy ŌĆö never a blocking dialog.

### 10.3 The five example workflows (each GUI-first AND CLI-visible)

1. **Beginner review** ŌĆö drop a PGN ŌåÆ step moves ŌåÆ each position shows grounded `position describe` + `engine analyze`; mistakes flagged. *Depends on C* for automatic mistakeŌåÆstudy routing; until C lands, this is manual stepping with per-position analysis (already possible). The exact `crtk` command is always shown.
2. **Research / ML** ŌĆö Datasets loads an export, shows label distribution + bad-row count, builds `record dataset lc0 ŌĆ” --weights ŌĆ”` with budgets visible; the run manifest captures input/output SHA-256.
3. **Publishing** ŌĆö Publish loads a `.book.toml`, live preview, `--check` dry-run, `book render`/`book cover`; output goes to the shared Run/output bus.
4. **Study** ŌĆö Board/Study + ECO opening tree ŌåÆ author a study from the current line ŌåÆ `book study` export.
5. **Database** ŌĆö load a PGN ŌåÆ index/filter/dedupe. *Depends on A* to become a persistent, queryable store with a `crtk pgn` CLI peer; today it is a per-session viewer only.

### 10.4 The mirror guarantee (why the GUI can never fork the core)

This is the load-bearing invariant, restated from 8H so it is not lost: (1) anything that *executes a command* spawns the real CLI child JVM; (2) [WorkbenchCommandRegression.java](src/testing/WorkbenchCommandRegression.java) walks `CliRegistry.root()` and asserts the "All CLI" template covers every runnable path; (3) once F's `crtk help --json` exists, the mirror should consume *that* catalog (the actual installed CLI) rather than reflecting in-process; (4) anything that *writes a persisted artifact* must route through the CLI ŌĆö a new structure test bans `chess.io.*` writers from the GUI packages so provenance and determinism live in one place. The persona/first-run/deep-link/command-preview-budget-visibility work, the `EXPECTED_FEATURE_PACKAGES` coverage gap (`draw`/`engine`/`play`/`relations` omitted), and the stale [wiki/workbench.md](wiki/workbench.md) (12 tabs vs shipped 8) are the bounded items worth doing *before* A/C/F land, because they make the existing power legible without competing for the foundation's budget. See **[Section 8H](#8h-workbench-productization-and-section-10-redesign-detail)** for the full testing plan and acceptance criteria.

---

## 11. Data & schema plan

This section specifies the on-disk and on-the-wire data contracts that the product-foundation work (Section 8: themes **F**, **A**, **C**, **D**, **I**) stands on. It is deliberately field-level but not full-JSON: it names keys and types, the nullability/required rules, and the validation/versioning/regression machinery that keeps every contract honest.

The governing principle is inherited from [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) and [tag/SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md): **one canonical, deterministic shape per artifact, derivable and re-emittable byte-identically.** Every schema below extends that discipline rather than inventing a parallel one. Where a shape already exists in source, this plan extends it additively and never silently changes a field's meaning.

Cross-reference: this is the data half of **Section 8F (Schemas & validation)**. 8F owns the *command-catalog* and *validation-command* surface; this section owns the *artifact field shapes* those commands validate. The two are co-dependent: `crtk help --json` (8F) describes commands; the schemas here describe their inputs and outputs. Neither ships meaningfully without the other.

---

### 11.1 The schema-version problem we are fixing

Verified against source: [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) has a fixed 7-field shape (`created`, `engine`, `parent`, `position`, `description`, `tags`, `analysis`) and **no `schema_version` field** (confirmed lines 17ŌĆō26, 39ŌĆō74). The only versioned artifact in the entire repo is [RunManifest.java](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java), which uses the string constant `"crtk.workbench.run-manifest.v1"`. The two exporter sidecars that *do* exist ŌĆö `<stem>.lc0.meta.json` ([RecordLc0Exporter.java](src/chess/io/RecordLc0Exporter.java):110) and `<stem>.classifier.meta.json` ([ClassifierDatasetExporter.java](src/chess/io/ClassifierDatasetExporter.java):275) ŌĆö carry encoder/shape/label fields but **no version, no git commit, no input checksum** (confirmed: `writeMetadata` starts at `ClassifierDatasetExporter.java`:525 and its highest field is `recommended_pos_weight`; there is no version key). And `record dataset npy` ([RecordDatasetExporter.java](src/chess/io/RecordDatasetExporter.java)) writes **no sidecar at all**.

Every new schema below therefore carries an explicit version, and we retrofit one onto `Record`.

---

### 11.2 Schema-version policy (applies to every artifact)

**Naming.** Reuse the existing `RunManifest` convention verbatim. Every versioned artifact carries a string field named `schema` with the value `crtk.<artifact>.v<major>` ŌĆö e.g. `crtk.record.v2`, `crtk.review-row.v1`, `crtk.dataset-manifest.v1`. This is a literal, greppable string, not a parsed semver tuple, matching `RunManifest.SCHEMA`. (ASSUMPTION: a single integer major is sufficient; we do not need minor/patch on-disk because additive changes do not bump the major ŌĆö see below.)

**Compatibility rules:**

| Change | Major bump? | Reader behavior |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Add an optional field | No | Old readers ignore unknown keys (already the de-facto behavior of `Json.parseStringField`, which reads named fields and ignores the rest) |
| Add a required field | Yes | Old readers reject `v(n+1)` loudly |
| Rename / retype / remove a field | Yes | Old readers reject `v(n+1)` loudly |
| Change a field's *semantics* (same name/type) | Yes (this is the dangerous one) | ŌĆö |

**The hard rule, grounded in [tag/SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md):** the tag-line grammar is the one contract that is *not* gated behind a version number, because it is re-derivable from the FEN. Instead it is gated behind golden fixtures (`testdata/tags/*.tsv`). New tag families/motifs are additive vocabulary, registered in `chess.tag.core.Literals` and `chess.tag.Sort` per the existing extension procedure (SCHEMA.md ┬¦"Extending the schema"). A tag *family* that changes the meaning of an existing key is a breaking change and must be caught by the fixture diff, not a version bump.

**Reader contract.** A reader presented with an unknown major MUST fail loudly with the artifact path and the version it saw versus the versions it supports. This is the inverse of today's tolerant-drop behavior in `Record.fromJson` (returns `null` on a bad FEN, [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java):474, 484) and `RecordIO` (silently counts-and-skips). We keep tolerant parsing for *missing optional* fields; we forbid it for *version mismatch*.

---

### 11.3 Record schema ŌĆö `crtk.record.v2`

The base unit. v2 = current 7 fields (unchanged meaning) **+ schema version + game/provenance linkage** that A and C need and that the digest flagged absent. The current shape is preserved exactly so existing `.record` files parse as implicit v1.

**Existing fields (carried forward, byte-identical meaning):**

| Field | Type | Required | Source |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `created` | long (epoch ms UTC) | yes | [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java):44 |
| `engine` | string \| null | no | engine name+version, e.g. `"Stockfish 16"` |
| `parent` | string (FEN) \| null | no | parent position FEN |
| `position` | string (FEN) \| null | no | analyzed position FEN |
| `description` | string (`""` if unset, never null) | yes | free-form |
| `tags` | string[] | yes (may be `[]`) | tag-line strings per [tag/SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md) |
| `analysis` | string[] (UCI info lines) | yes (may be `[]`) | `chess.uci.Analysis` lines |

**New v2 fields (all optional ŌåÆ no major bump needed beyond the `schema` key itself; we bump to v2 because `schema` is the first *required* addition):**

| Field | Type | Required | Why |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | string `"crtk.record.v2"` | yes (v2 only) | version gate; absence ŌćÆ treated as v1 |
| `id` | string | no | stable record id; **derive deterministically**, do not random-generate. Use `position.signatureCore()` hex (the FNV-1a digest, [Position.java](src/chess/core/Position.java):457) so the same position yields the same id ŌĆö this is what dedupe and cross-export joins need and is the only collision-tolerant key the core already exposes |
| `game_id` | string \| null | no | links a record to a stored game (theme A); today `training-jsonl` hard-codes this null |
| `ply` | int \| null | no | half-move index within `game_id`; null for standalone records |
| `source` | object \| null | no | provenance: `{kind: "mine"\|"pgn-import"\|"review"\|"manual", file: string\|null, file_sha256: string\|null}` |

**Determinism note.** `Record.equals`/`hashCode` deliberately exclude `analysis` ([Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java):526ŌĆō532). v2 must NOT add `id`/`game_id` to `equals` without thought: `id` is *derived from* `position`, which is already in `equals`, so adding it is redundant but harmless; `game_id`/`ply`/`source` are provenance and should be excluded from `equals` so that the same position mined twice from different games still compares equal (preserving the existing dedupe semantics). This is a real design decision, not a default ŌĆö flag it in the v2 Javadoc.

---

### 11.4 Tag schema ŌĆö line grammar, unchanged; dynamic-family registration, fixed

The tag contract is already authoritative in [tag/SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md) and does not get a JSON version number ŌĆö it is a *line grammar* (`FAMILY: key=value key=value`), sorted by `chess.tag.Sort` and de-duplicated, byte-stable per FEN (SCHEMA.md ┬¦"Design contract" rules 1ŌĆō3).

**No change to the grammar.** What this plan *does* fix is the structural gap the digest verified: the dynamic game-analysis families (`MOVE_EFFECT`, `LINE`, `VARIATION`, `GAME`) are emitted via inline string literals (e.g. `"MOVE_EFFECT: san="` in [MoveEffect.java](src/chess/tag/MoveEffect.java):45) and are **absent from `Sort.FAMILY_ORDER` (20 static families only) and from `chess.tag.core.Literals`**. Consequence: they bypass canonical sort/dedupe/delta/Filter. The schema work for C (review router) requires registering them:

- Add the four families to `chess.tag.Sort.FAMILY_ORDER` (after `GAME`'s natural rank ŌĆö they are whole-line/whole-game families, so they sort *after* the position families).
- Add their prefix literals to `chess.tag.core.Literals`.
- Document them in [tag/SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md) (currently only in `tag/GAME_ANALYSIS.md`).

**Delta JSONL shape (already exists, formalize as `crtk.tag-delta.v1`).** From SCHEMA.md ┬¦"Per-move deltas", the `fen tags --sequence --delta` row is:

| Field | Type |
| --- | --- |
| `index` | int |
| `parent` / `fen` | string (FEN) |
| `move_uci` / `move_san` | string \| null |
| `tags` | string[] (sorted) |
| `delta` | object \| null: `{added: string[], removed: string[], changed: [{key, from, to}]}` |

This shape feeds the review-row schema below.

---

### 11.5 Review-row schema ŌĆö `crtk.review-row.v1` (theme C)

One JSONL row per analyzed move of a reviewed game. This is the new artifact C produces; it has no predecessor in source, so it is greenfield and gets v1. It is the bridge from a stored game (A) to study tasks (D).

| Field | Type | Required | Source / grounding |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | `"crtk.review-row.v1"` | yes | version gate |
| `game_id` | string | yes | FK into the game store (A) |
| `ply` | int | yes | half-move index |
| `fen_before` / `fen_after` | string (FEN) | yes | positions around the move |
| `move_uci` / `move_san` | string | yes | the move actually played |
| `eval_before_cp` / `eval_after_cp` | int \| null | no | from `record analysis-delta`'s eval samples |
| `mate_before` / `mate_after` | int \| null | no | signed mate distance |
| `delta_cp` | int \| null | no | eval swing (positive = side-to-move gained) |
| `classification` | enum string | yes | `best \| good \| inaccuracy \| mistake \| blunder \| forced \| book` |
| `best_move_uci` / `best_move_san` | string \| null | no | engine's preferred move |
| `refutation_pv` | string[] (UCI) \| null | no | the line that punishes a mistake ŌĆö **the seed for a study task** |
| `move_effect_tags` | string[] | no | the registered `MOVE_EFFECT:` lines (11.4) for this move |
| `turning_point` | bool | no | gated; see caveat |

**Hard caveat, grounded in the digest's fact-check:** `classification` and `turning_point` depend on engine-graded verdicts. The digest confirmed `MOVE_EFFECT quality=`/`turning_point` are **deferred/unimplemented** in the tag engine. Therefore v1 of this schema MUST source `classification` either (a) from an external UCI engine via [Engine.java](src/chess/uci/Engine.java) + [Pool.java](src/application/Pool.java), recording the engine id/budget in the row's provenance, or (b) leave it `forced`/`book` for the trivially-derivable cases. Do not present a hand-tuned static classification as engine-grade. (ASSUMPTION: external-UCI grading is the v1 path, since that is the repo's documented "reference-grade" route.)

---

### 11.6 Study-task schema ŌĆö `crtk.study-task.v1` (themes C ŌåÆ D)

A study task is a self-contained, gradeable unit produced by the review router and consumable by the SRS (D). It is what `record export` for study would emit. Greenfield, v1.

| Field | Type | Required | Grounding |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | `"crtk.study-task.v1"` | yes | ŌĆö |
| `id` | string | yes | derived from `position.signatureCore()` hex + task `kind` |
| `kind` | enum string | yes | `find_refutation \| best_move \| only_move \| recall_plan \| endgame_technique` |
| `position` | string (FEN) | yes | the prompt position |
| `solution` | string[] (UCI) | yes | the line that solves it (validated by replaying through the core, per the book-validator precedent) |
| `alt_solutions` | string[][] \| null | no | accepted alternates |
| `goal` | enum string | yes | `win \| draw \| defend \| convert` (reuse `chess.puzzle.Goal` WIN/DRAW/UNKNOWN vocabulary) |
| `rating` | int \| null | no | from `chess.puzzle.Scorer` (note: corpus-internal, NOT human Elo ŌĆö must be labeled as such, matching the existing `Difficulty` caveat) |
| `tags` | string[] | no | grounded tag lines explaining the motif |
| `explanation` | string \| null | no | from `position describe` (classical, faithful-by-construction) ŌĆö see G |
| `provenance` | object | yes | `{from_game_id, ply, review_row_schema, engine_id, engine_budget}` |

**Reuse, not reinvention.** `solution`-validation borrows the exact pattern from `BookValidator`/`StudyBookValidator` (replay every move via `Move.isMove` then `SAN.fromAlgebraic`). `rating`/`goal` reuse `chess.puzzle.Scorer`/`Goal`. `explanation` reuses the deterministic [ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java), which cannot hallucinate. This keeps study tasks inside the one-shared-core, grounded-explanations values.

---

### 11.7 Repertoire-item schema ŌĆö `crtk.repertoire-item.v1` (theme D)

A repertoire line + the SRS scheduling state attached to a position the user is responsible for knowing. Greenfield, v1. D is explicitly sequenced *after* A/C/F/G in Section 8, so this schema is a forward declaration ŌĆö but pinning it now prevents A's game store from being built in a way that can't host it.

| Field | Type | Required | Grounding |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | `"crtk.repertoire-item.v1"` | yes | ŌĆö |
| `id` | string | yes | derived from `position.signatureCore()` |
| `position` | string (FEN) | yes | the position to recall from |
| `expected_move_uci` / `expected_move_san` | string | yes | the repertoire move |
| `side` | enum `white \| black` | yes | whose repertoire this belongs to |
| `eco` / `opening_name` | string \| null | no | from `chess.eco.Encyclopedia` (the bundled 3,412-entry complete A00-E99 book) |
| `line_id` | string | yes | groups items belonging to one named line |
| `parent_id` | string \| null | no | tree linkage for transpositions (keyed on `signatureCore`, matching how `Encyclopedia` does counter-insensitive lookup) |
| `srs` | object | yes | scheduling state ŌĆö see below |
| `provenance` | object | no | `{from_study_task_id, from_game_id}` |

**SRS sub-object (`srs`), the only stateful/mutable part of any schema here:**

| Field | Type | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `algorithm` | string `"sm2"` | (ASSUMPTION: SM-2 is the v1 scheduler; it is the simplest deterministic choice and has no third-party dep) |
| `interval_days` | double | current interval |
| `ease` | double | SM-2 ease factor |
| `reps` | int | successful repetitions |
| `due` | long (epoch ms UTC) | next review time |
| `last_reviewed` | long \| null | epoch ms |
| `history` | `[{ts, grade}]` | append-only review log |

**Determinism tension to flag:** every other schema here is a pure function of inputs and is byte-reproducible. Repertoire `srs` state is inherently mutable and time-dependent (`due`, `last_reviewed`). It therefore CANNOT participate in the golden-output regression strategy (11.13) the way the others do. Its regression coverage is *transition* coverage ŌĆö given state X and grade G at time T, assert next state Y ŌĆö not byte-equality of a file. This is the one schema that breaks the "diff two runs" rule, and that must be documented, not glossed.

---

### 11.8 Database manifest ŌĆö `crtk.db-manifest.v1` (theme A)

The index/header for a local PGN game store. The store itself is JSONL `.record`/game rows (per 8A's "JSONL-backed store keyed on game-id + `signatureCore`"); the manifest is the queryable index that makes it a database rather than a flat file. Greenfield, v1.

| Field | Type | Required | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | `"crtk.db-manifest.v1"` | yes | ŌĆö |
| `created` / `updated` | long (epoch ms) | yes | ŌĆö |
| `crtk_version` | string | yes | from `VersionCommand.VERSION` |
| `game_count` | int | yes | ŌĆö |
| `position_count` | int | yes | distinct `signatureCore` keys |
| `shards` | `[{path, sha256, game_count, byte_size}]` | yes | the JSONL data files this manifest indexes |
| `position_index` | `{path, sha256}` \| null | no | sidecar mapping `signatureCore` ŌåÆ `[{game_id, ply}]`; the thing that makes position-search O(1) |
| `games` | `[{game_id, white, black, result, date, event, eco, ply_count, source}]` | yes | per-game header rows (the searchable card layer) |

**Provenance is mandatory here** because A is a long-lived store, not a one-shot export. `crtk_version` + per-shard `sha256` is the minimum to detect corruption and version drift ŌĆö exactly the provenance the digest found *missing* from every current dataset sidecar. Reuse `RunManifest.sha256(Path)` ([RunManifest.java](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java):427) ŌĆö do not write a second SHA-256 helper.

---

### 11.9 Import manifest ŌĆö `crtk.import-manifest.v1` (theme A; theme B later, boundary-gated)

Records what an `import` operation ingested, for auditability and idempotent re-import. Greenfield, v1. B (platform import) is deferred and boundary-gated to **read-only file/public-export ingestion only**; this manifest serves the in-boundary `pgn import <file>` first, and a future read-only fetch reuses it unchanged.

| Field | Type | Required | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | `"crtk.import-manifest.v1"` | yes | ŌĆö |
| `imported_at` | long (epoch ms) | yes | ŌĆö |
| `crtk_version` | string | yes | ŌĆö |
| `source` | object | yes | `{kind: "pgn-file"\|"folder"\|"public-export", path\|url: string, sha256: string\|null}` ŌĆö note `url` is permitted ONLY for read-only public exports; account linking is out of scope per the product boundary |
| `games_seen` / `games_imported` / `games_skipped` | int | yes | counts |
| `skipped` | `[{reason, line_or_game}]` | no | **fail-loud, not silent-drop** ŌĆö the explicit fix for the tolerant-drop debt the digest flagged in `Reader`/`Record.fromJson` |
| `assigned_game_ids` | string[] | yes | the `game_id`s minted on import (deterministic: hash of normalized headers + mainline) |
| `target_db` | string | yes | path of the `crtk.db-manifest.v1` the games landed in |

---

### 11.10 Dataset manifest ŌĆö `crtk.dataset-manifest.v1` (theme I)

The single sidecar that fixes the verified provenance gaps: `npy` has no sidecar; `lc0`/`classifier` sidecars lack version/git/checksums; the wiki claims byte-exact determinism the sidecars cannot prove. This schema is written by *every* exporter (`npy`, `lc0`, `classifier`, `training-jsonl`, `puzzle-jsonl`, `puzzle-elo-jsonl`), unifying what is today three inconsistent ad-hoc shapes.

| Field | Type | Required | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | `"crtk.dataset-manifest.v1"` | yes | ŌĆö |
| `created` | long (epoch ms) | yes | ŌĆö |
| `crtk_version` | string | yes | `VersionCommand.VERSION` |
| `git_commit` | string \| null | yes (null only if unavailable) | the provenance the digest found missing everywhere |
| `command` | string[] | yes | the exact argv that produced this dataset (reuse `RunManifest`'s `args[]` idea) |
| `exporter` | enum string | yes | `npy \| lc0 \| classifier \| training-jsonl \| puzzle-jsonl \| puzzle-elo-jsonl` |
| `inputs` | `[{path, sha256, byte_size}]` | yes | input record files, checksummed |
| `weights` | `{path, sha256}` \| null | no | for `lc0`/`puzzle-jsonl` which require a `.bin` net ŌĆö checksum the model |
| `outputs` | `[{path, sha256, shape, dtype}]` | yes | the produced tensors/JSONL, checksummed |
| `encoding` | object | yes | the *existing* per-exporter encoding block, lifted verbatim (e.g. classifier's `{encoder: "classifier-21planes", planes: 21, squares: 64, order, side_to_move_perspective}` from [ClassifierDatasetExporter.java](src/chess/io/ClassifierDatasetExporter.java):554ŌĆō561) |
| `labels` | object \| null | no | existing label block (`target`, `positive_definition`, `recommended_pos_weight`, filter DSLs) |
| `filter_dsl` / `label_filter_dsl` | string \| null | no | the `chess.uci.Filter` DSL strings used for row/label selection |

**Migration, not replacement.** The existing `<stem>.lc0.meta.json` and `<stem>.classifier.meta.json` become `crtk.dataset-manifest.v1` documents (same filenames, superset content). `npy` gains one. This is additive: an old reader of the lc0 meta still finds `encoding`/`labels`; a new reader also finds `git_commit`/checksums.

**Also fix in this theme (verified bug, not schema):** `chess.nn.classifier.Model.DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` points at `models/classifier_...bin` but the shipped file is `models/puzzle-classifier_...bin` ŌĆö `loadDefault()` is broken out of the box. Track it alongside the manifest work since both live in the dataset/ML provenance theme.

---

### 11.11 Book manifest ŌĆö `crtk.book-manifest.v1` (publishing; already partly real)

The book pipeline already has two imperative manifest models ŌĆö `chess.book.model.Book` (puzzle-grid) and `chess.book.model.StudyBook` (compositions), loadable as JSON *or* TOML. They are validated by `BookValidator`/`StudyBookValidator` (every FEN parsed, every solution move replayed). What is missing, per the digest, is a *declared* schema: there is no JSON Schema file, so external tools and the Workbench cannot validate a manifest against a published contract. This schema *describes the existing shape* ŌĆö it does not change it.

**Book (puzzle-grid) ŌĆö key fields (from `chess.book.model.Book`):**

| Field | Type | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `schema` | `"crtk.book-manifest.v1"` | **new** ŌĆö the one additive field; absence ŌćÆ legacy |
| `title` / `subtitle` / `author` / `time` / `location` / `language` | string | metadata |
| `pages` | int | ŌĆö |
| `tablefrequency` / `puzzlerows` / `puzzlecolumns` | int | layout |
| `paperwidth` / `paperheight` / `innermargin` / `outermargin` / `topmargin` / `bottommargin` | double (cm) | physical layout; cmŌåÆpt = 72/2.54 |
| `imprint` / `dedication` / `introduction` / `howToRead` / `blurb` / `link` / `afterword` | string[] | front/back matter |
| `elements` | `[{position: FEN, moves: SAN/UCI line}]` | the puzzles; `moves` validated by replay |

**StudyBook ŌĆö distinct key fields:** `pageSize` (`a4\|a5\|letter`), `margin` (pt), `diagramsPerRow`, `boardPixels`, `whiteSideDown`, `showFen`, and `compositions[]` with index-aligned `figureFens[]`/`figureMovesAlgebraic[]`/`figureArrows[]` plus `hintLevel1..4`.

**Determinism caveat the schema cannot fix but must document:** book *output* byte-stability depends on installed AWT fonts and a hardcoded `/usr/share/texmf/...` Latin Modern path ([Font.java](src/chess/pdf/document/Font.java)), and `Document.escape()` maps non-ASCII ŌåÆ `?`. The manifest is deterministic; the rendered PDF is environment-dependent. The schema doc must state this so "byte-stable diagrams" is not over-claimed.

---

### 11.12 Validation commands (the 8F surface, applied to these schemas)

8F introduces the machine-readable command catalog and a `crtk validate` family. Concretely, against the schemas above:

- **`crtk schema list`** ŌĆö emit the registry of known schema ids and their current versions (serialized, like `crtk help --json`).
- **`crtk schema show <id>`** ŌĆö emit the JSON Schema document for one artifact (e.g. `crtk.record.v2`). These JSON Schema files are the *first* `*.schema.json` artifacts in the repo (the fact-check confirmed zero exist today). They live under `schema/` and are themselves regression-checked against the emitting code.
- **`crtk validate record <file>`** / **`crtk validate dataset <file>`** / **`crtk validate db <file>`** etc. ŌĆö strict validation that **fails loudly** with `{path, line, reason}` rather than the current silent-skip. Exit code 2 on schema violation (reusing the existing usage-error code from `Validation.java`/`CommandFailure`), 3 on file-not-found (matching `CommandSupport.parsePositionOrExit`'s invalid-FEN exit-3 convention).
- **Strict streaming mode for `RecordIO`** ŌĆö a flag that turns the current count-and-drop ([RecordIO](src/application/cli/RecordIO.java) silent skip) into a per-line error report, so a schema-drifted `.record` fails the import instead of quietly shrinking the dataset.

These reuse `CliRegistry` metadata and the `Validation.java`/`CommandFailure` exit-code machinery rather than inventing a validator framework ŌĆö consistent with the no-third-party-deps value.

---

### 11.13 Regression strategy: schemas tied to deterministic golden outputs

The repo's testing culture is golden-value-in-source + the one TSV fixture (`testdata/tags/static.tsv`), with **no JaCoCo/coverage and no byte-equality determinism test** (digest-confirmed: regressions assert size thresholds and substrings, not byte-identity). The schema work must not perpetuate that gap. Strategy, in dependency order:

1. **Schema-vs-emitter parity test (new).** For each schema, a regression that (a) loads `schema/crtk.<artifact>.v<n>.schema.json`, (b) generates a sample artifact from a fixed input through the real emitter, and (c) asserts the artifact validates against the schema. This is the test that catches "the code added a field but nobody updated the schema" ŌĆö the exact drift the digest found between `Model.DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` and the shipped filename, and between the dynamic tag families and `Sort`/`Literals`.

2. **Byte-equality determinism test (new, fills a verified gap).** Run each *deterministic* exporter twice from the same fixed inputs and assert the two outputs are byte-identical, with one explicit normalization: **strip the time-dependent fields** (`created`, `imported_at`, `updated`, and `git_commit` if it varies) before comparing. This is necessary because, like `Result.equals` including `elapsedMillis` (digest-confirmed foot-gun), naive whole-file equality would flake on the `created` timestamp. The test codifies *which* fields are excluded from determinism ŌĆö making the determinism claim precise instead of aspirational.

3. **Golden fixtures for the new artifacts.** Extend the `testdata/` corpus beyond the single tag TSV: add a small fixed game ŌåÆ its `crtk.review-row.v1` JSONL ŌåÆ its `crtk.study-task.v1` rows, stored as golden files. A change to the router or schema that alters any field is then a visible diff in the PR. (This directly serves theme C's regression need.)

4. **Tag-family fixture extension.** Registering `MOVE_EFFECT`/`LINE`/`VARIATION`/`GAME` in `Sort`/`Literals` (11.4) requires a golden `--analyze-game` output added to the fixture set, since these families currently bypass the sorted/deduped pipeline and have no fixture coverage.

5. **SRS is the exception.** As noted in 11.7, repertoire `srs` state is mutable and time-dependent. Its regression is a *state-transition table* (input state + grade ŌåÆ expected next state, with `due`/`last_reviewed` computed from a fixed injected `now`), not a byte-equality golden. Document this explicitly so a future contributor does not "fix" the missing byte-golden by adding a flaky one.

6. **Wire the orphans in.** The digest verified that `RecordTrainingJSONLRegressionTest` and `RecordLC0ExporterRegressionTest` exist but are **not referenced by `run_regression_suite.sh`** ŌĆö they pass by not running. Any schema work on the dataset exporters MUST add these (and the new schema-parity tests) to the `cli`/`core` suite targets, or the green bar is lying about ML provenance coverage.

---

### 11.14 Summary: dependency order of the schema work

Grounded in the Section 8 verdicts (F is P0; A/C/I are P1 build-now; D is P2 build-later):

1. **F first** ŌĆö `schema` version policy (11.2), `crtk.record.v2` (11.3), JSON Schema files + `crtk schema`/`crtk validate` (11.12), schema-parity + byte-determinism tests (11.13 steps 1ŌĆō2). Nothing else has a stable contract until this lands.
2. **I alongside** ŌĆö `crtk.dataset-manifest.v1` (11.10) retrofitting the three existing/missing sidecars; fix the classifier `DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` bug; wire in the orphan tests.
3. **A** ŌĆö `crtk.db-manifest.v1` (11.8) + `crtk.import-manifest.v1` (11.9), built on the `Record v2` `game_id`/`id` linkage; tag-family registration (11.4) so stored-game annotation is canonical.
4. **C** ŌĆö `crtk.review-row.v1` (11.5) + `crtk.study-task.v1` (11.6) + the C golden fixtures (11.13 step 3), gated on external-UCI grading for `classification`.
5. **D (later)** ŌĆö `crtk.repertoire-item.v1` (11.7) with the SRS state-transition regression (11.13 step 5).
6. **Publishing (independent)** ŌĆö `crtk.book-manifest.v1` (11.11) is a *documentation* of an existing shape; low-cost, can land any time once the schema-parity harness (11.13 step 1) exists.

Every artifact carries a literal `schema` string, fails loudly on unknown major, excludes time-fields from determinism comparison, and reuses the existing `signatureCore` keying, `RunManifest.sha256`, `Validation`/`CommandFailure` exit codes, and `BookValidator`-style move-replay validation. No new framework, no third-party dependency, one canonical shape per artifact ŌĆö the same discipline [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) and [tag/SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md) already enforce.

---

## 12. Game-review-to-study pipeline

This section specifies the **game-review-to-study router** as an 11-stage pipeline of
already-shipped CRTK commands plus the *one* new orchestrating verb that does not yet
exist. It is the concrete realization of theme **8C** (game-review-to-study router,
verdict `build-now`, P1), and it consumes the schema/provenance work of **8I**
(dataset provenance / ML exports, P1) and feeds the explanation deepening of **8G**
(grounded explanations, P1). It is the substrate **8D** (repertoire/SRS) is built on.

### Status of the building blocks (grounded)
