### Milestone M1 ŌĆö Foundations & schemas (theme F)

The precondition for E (SDK), K (editor tooling), A/C (on-disk stores), I (provenance). Reuse the metadata already in [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) and the [RunManifest.java](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java) schema-string + SHA-256 pattern rather than inventing new conventions.

#### M1-1 ŌĆö `crtk help --json` machine-readable command catalog
**Priority:** P0
**Context:** [HelpCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/HelpCommand.java) is 83 KB of human prose; there is no machine-readable command catalog even though [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) holds every path/alias/summary/example/related in memory. Agents and editor tooling must scrape prose today.
**Implementation notes:** Add a `--json` mode to `help` that walks `CliRegistry.root()` and emits `{schemaVersion, areas:[{path, aliases, summary, about, usageTail, examples[], runnable, children:[...]}]}`. Use `utility.Json`. Do not duplicate the tree ŌĆö serialize the existing `CliCommand` nodes (`commandPath()`, `aliasPaths()`, `isRunnable()`).
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] `crtk help --json` emits one stable JSON object covering every runnable path and alias.
- [x] Output is byte-deterministic across runs (sorted children, no timestamps).
- [x] Excludes the workbench launcher nested tree as `WorkbenchCommandRegression` already does.
**Tests to run:** new `testing.CommandCatalogRegressionTest` asserting every `CliRegistry` runnable path appears; run via `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [ai-agents.md](wiki/ai-agents.md), [command-reference.md](wiki/command-reference.md).
**Labels:** `cli`, `schema`, `agents`, `P0`.

#### M1-2 ŌĆö Add `schemaVersion` to the Record struct
**Priority:** P0
**Context:** [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) has a fixed 7-field shape with no version field. Any future migration (game-id, provenance) is unsafe without one.
**Implementation notes:** Add an optional `schemaVersion` (int, default 1) to `Record`, serialized in `toJson()` and tolerantly parsed in `fromJson()` (absent ŌćÆ 1). Keep `equals()/hashCode()` keys unchanged to avoid breaking dedupe semantics. Update [RecordIO.java](src/application/cli/RecordIO.java) streaming if needed.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Old `.record` files (no version field) still parse as version 1.
- [x] New writes include `schemaVersion`.
- [x] Round-trip (`toJson` ŌåÆ `fromJson`) preserves the field.
**Tests to run:** `testing.JsonRegressionTest`, `testing.PGNRegressionTest`, plus a Record round-trip test; `./scripts/run_regression_suite.sh core cli`.
**Docs to update:** [datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md), [outputs-and-logs.md](wiki/outputs-and-logs.md).
**Labels:** `schema`, `records`, `P0`.

#### M1-3 ŌĆö Publish JSON Schema files for the stable on-disk contracts
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** No `*.schema.json` exist anywhere; contracts live only in prose and golden assertions. SDK/editor consumers (E, K) need validatable schemas.
**Implementation notes:** Add a `schemas/` directory with JSON Schema (draft 2020-12) files for: `.record` object, `training-jsonl` row, `analysis-delta` row, dataset `meta.json` (lc0/classifier). Derive field lists from [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java), [RecordTrainingJsonlCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/RecordTrainingJsonlCommand.java), [RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java), [ClassifierDatasetExporter.java](src/chess/io/ClassifierDatasetExporter.java), [RecordLc0Exporter.java](src/chess/io/RecordLc0Exporter.java). No runtime dependency ŌĆö schemas are reference artifacts.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] Schema files exist for record, training-jsonl, analysis-delta, dataset meta.json.
- [ ] Each schema's `$id` carries the `schemaVersion`.
- [ ] A regression test validates a sample emitted file against its schema using the in-house `utility.Json` (no third-party validator) ŌĆö at minimum field-presence/type checks.
**Tests to run:** new `testing.SchemaRegressionTest` under `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md), [ai-agents.md](wiki/ai-agents.md).
**Labels:** `schema`, `datasets`, `P1`.

#### M1-4 ŌĆö Fail-loud strict mode for record/JSONL ingestion
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) `fromJson` and [Reader.java](src/chess/io/Reader.java) silently drop malformed input (return null/skip), so corrupt or schema-drifted files lose data quietly ŌĆö bad for reproducible datasets.
**Implementation notes:** Add a `--strict` flag to `record files` / exporters (parsed in [RecordCommands.java](src/application/cli/command/RecordCommands.java)) that routes through a strict streaming path in [RecordIO.java](src/application/cli/RecordIO.java): on the first invalid object, emit a per-line error to stderr and exit non-zero (use exit code 3, the existing input-error code). Default behavior unchanged (tolerant) for backward compatibility.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] `record files --strict` on a file with one bad object exits 3 and names the offending index on stderr.
- [ ] Without `--strict`, behavior is unchanged (counted-and-skipped).
**Tests to run:** `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest` (add strict-mode cases); `./scripts/run_regression_suite.sh cli`.
**Docs to update:** [outputs-and-logs.md](wiki/outputs-and-logs.md), [ai-agents.md](wiki/ai-agents.md).
**Labels:** `cli`, `records`, `validation`, `P1`.

#### M1-5 ŌĆö `crtk schema` discovery verb
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** With schemas published (M1-3), agents need a way to retrieve them without filesystem knowledge.
**Implementation notes:** Add a `schema` leaf to [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java): `crtk schema list` and `crtk schema show <name>` emitting the embedded schema JSON. Embed schema text as resources compiled into the jar so it works from the installed launcher.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] `crtk schema list` enumerates available schema names.
- [ ] `crtk schema show record` prints valid JSON Schema.
**Tests to run:** `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest`; `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [command-reference.md](wiki/command-reference.md), [ai-agents.md](wiki/ai-agents.md).
**Labels:** `cli`, `schema`, `agents`, `P2`.

---

### Milestone M2 ŌĆö Import + local PGN database (themes A, B)

The biggest study-foundation gap. Promote the in-memory logic in [PgnExplorerModel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) into `chess.*` core so CLI and Workbench share it (preserves one-shared-core). Depends on M1 schema/version work.

#### M2-1 ŌĆö `chess.pgn.store` core: on-disk game store format + index
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** [Pgn.java](src/chess/struct/Pgn.java)/[Game.java](src/chess/struct/Game.java) parse and round-trip games but there is no persistent, indexed store; everything is stateless conversion.
**Implementation notes:** New `chess.pgn` (or `chess.db`) package: a JSONL/.record-backed store with a sidecar index keyed on a stable `gameId` (hash of tags+mainline) and per-position `signatureCore()` ([Position.java](src/chess/core/Position.java)). Reuse [Writer.java](src/chess/io/Writer.java) append-safe writes and [Reader.java](src/chess/io/Reader.java). Add `gameId`/provenance fields (depends on M1-2 `schemaVersion`). Keep it a pure library with no CLI yet.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] Importing the same PGN twice is idempotent (dedup by `gameId`).
- [ ] Position-signature index returns all games containing a given FEN.
- [ ] Store format has a documented schema and version.
**Tests to run:** new `testing.PgnStoreRegressionTest` under `core`.
**Docs to update:** [datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md); new `wiki/pgn-database.md`.
**Labels:** `pgn-db`, `core`, `P1`.

#### M2-2 ŌĆö `crtk pgn import` (file/folder, read-only)
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** No CLI ingests a user's own games into a store. Folder import is the in-boundary slice of theme B (read-only, local files; **no** account linking/sync/social).
**Implementation notes:** Add `pgn` area to [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) with `import` action: `--input` (file or dir), `--recursive`, `--store <path>`. Parse via [Pgn.java](src/chess/struct/Pgn.java), write via M2-1 store. Report imported/skipped/duplicate counts.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] `crtk pgn import -i games/ --recursive` imports all `.pgn` under the dir.
- [ ] Re-import is idempotent.
- [ ] Exit codes follow the 0/2/3 convention.
**Tests to run:** `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest` (add `pgn import` cases); `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [command-reference.md](wiki/command-reference.md), `wiki/pgn-database.md`.
**Labels:** `pgn-db`, `cli`, `import`, `P1`.

#### M2-3 ŌĆö `crtk pgn query` / `pgn show` / `pgn stats`
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** A store is only useful if queryable. The Workbench already has filter logic in [PgnExplorerModel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) to mirror.
**Implementation notes:** `pgn query` filters by player/event/date/result/ECO/position-FEN; `pgn show <gameId>` emits PGN or JSON; `pgn stats` summarizes the store. Reuse [Encyclopedia.java](src/chess/eco/Encyclopedia.java) for ECO labels. Output `--json`/`--jsonl`.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] `crtk pgn query --player "X" --json` returns matching game headers.
- [ ] `crtk pgn query --position <FEN>` uses the signature index.
- [ ] `pgn show` round-trips a stored game back to valid PGN.
**Tests to run:** `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest`, `testing.PGNRegressionTest`; `cli`.
**Docs to update:** `wiki/pgn-database.md`, [use-cases.md](wiki/use-cases.md).
**Labels:** `pgn-db`, `cli`, `P1`.

#### M2-4 ŌĆö Promote PgnExplorerModel onto the core store (Workbench)
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** [PgnExplorerModel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) duplicates index/filter logic in-memory. Once M2-1 lands, the GUI should read the same core store so CLI and Workbench cannot diverge.
**Implementation notes:** Refactor the Workbench PGN explorer to back onto the `chess.pgn` store API; keep the panel UI. This is a productization win that arrives almost free after M2-1.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] Workbench PGN explorer reads from a store opened by `crtk pgn import`.
- [ ] No duplicated index logic between GUI and core.
**Tests to run:** `testing.WorkbenchGameRegression` via headless `WorkbenchRegressionTest`.
**Docs to update:** [workbench.md](wiki/workbench.md).
**Labels:** `pgn-db`, `workbench`, `P2`.

---

### Milestone M3 ŌĆö Review ŌåÆ Study router (theme C)

Connect the existing grounded primitives into a router that turns mistakes into study units. Depends on A (game input), F (study-unit schema), and M0-7 (registered dynamic families).

#### M3-1 ŌĆö Engine-graded move verdicts (blunder/turning-point)
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** The MOVE_EFFECT/VARIATION families carry structure but the `quality=`/`turning_point`/`eval_swing` verdicts are deferred per [GAME_ANALYSIS.md](tag/GAME_ANALYSIS.md). A router needs graded verdicts to decide what to study.
**Implementation notes:** Compute per-move eval deltas by routing positions through an external UCI engine via [Engine.java](src/chess/uci/Engine.java) + [Pool.java](src/application/Pool.java) (reference-grade path) or the deterministic in-house search; attach `quality=`/`eval_swing`/`turning_point` to MOVE_EFFECT. Reuse drift logic from [RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java).
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [ ] A game with a known blunder yields a `quality=blunder` (or equivalent) MOVE_EFFECT at the right ply.
- [ ] Verdicts are deterministic for a fixed engine+budget.
**Tests to run:** `testing.TaggingRegressionTest` (add graded-verdict cases); `core` and `uci` (Stockfish-gated).
**Docs to update:** [tag/GAME_ANALYSIS.md](tag/GAME_ANALYSIS.md), [tag/SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md).
**Labels:** `review`, `tag-engine`, `P1`.

#### M3-2 ŌĆö Study-unit schema + emitter
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** No format ties a detected mistake to its refutation as a studiable unit.
**Implementation notes:** Define a study-unit JSON shape (game ref, ply, played move, refutation line, grounded tags, difficulty) as a JSON Schema (M1-3 pattern). Emit as `Record`s (the refutation position becomes a puzzle Record) reusing FENŌåÆpuzzle machinery from [MineCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/MineCommand.java).
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Study-unit schema published under `schemas/`.
- [x] Emitter produces a valid Record per detected turning point with the refutation as the puzzle.
**Tests to run:** new `testing.ReviewRouterRegressionTest`; `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md), new `wiki/review-to-study.md`.
**Labels:** `review`, `schema`, `P1`.

#### M3-3 ŌĆö `crtk review game` CLI verb
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** No verb ingests a game and emits study units; `puzzle mine` explicitly does not do "the human played X, study the refutation."
**Implementation notes:** Add `review` area (or `pgn review`) to [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java): `--pgn`/`--gameId`, engine budgets, `--threshold-cp`, output study units. Compose M3-1 verdicts + M3-2 emitter + [GameAnalyzer.java](src/chess/tag/game/GameAnalyzer.java). Mirror logic from [GameReviewPanel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/GameReviewPanel.java) and [PgnPrepReport.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnPrepReport.java).
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] `crtk review game --pgn g.pgn --to-study` emits one study unit per detected mistake.
- [x] Bounded by explicit engine budgets (`--max-nodes`/`--max-duration`).
**Tests to run:** `testing.ReviewRouterRegressionTest`, `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest`; `cli` + `uci`.
**Docs to update:** `wiki/review-to-study.md`, [use-cases.md](wiki/use-cases.md), [ai-agents.md](wiki/ai-agents.md).
**Labels:** `review`, `cli`, `P1`.

#### M3-4 ŌĆö Workbench Review surface backed by `crtk review`
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** [GameReviewPanel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/GameReviewPanel.java) does retry-jumps but not automated study-unit production.
**Implementation notes:** Add a "produce study units" action to the Review surface that shells the new CLI via [CommandRunner.java](src/application/gui/workbench/command/CommandRunner.java) and displays results, preserving CLI-is-source-of-truth.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Review surface can render CLI-produced review/study artifacts without recomputing verdicts.
- [x] Review surface produces and lists study units from the loaded game via the CLI.
**Tests to run:** `testing.WorkbenchGameRegression`.
**Docs to update:** [workbench.md](wiki/workbench.md).
**Labels:** `review`, `workbench`, `P2`.

---

### Milestone M4 ŌĆö Explanation depth (theme G)

Deepen the already-present grounded explanation layer. Depends on C (whole-game context) and the verification pass landing before any T5 wiring.

#### M4-1 ŌĆö Inference-time grounding/verification pass
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** [ARCHITECTURE.md](src/chess/describe/ARCHITECTURE.md) documents a verification pass (every SAN must be a legal candidate; eval/material/side consistency; fallback to classical on contradiction). Without it, wiring any T5 risks hallucination.
**Implementation notes:** `PositionDescriptionVerifier` checks generated text against [PositionDescriptionInput.java](src/chess/describe/PositionDescriptionInput.java): reject sentences naming non-candidate SANs, contradicting eval sign, or wrong side-to-move; on failure, regenerate or fall back to [ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java).
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Given a crafted hallucinated sentence, the verifier flags it and falls back to classical text.
- [x] Verified output never names a SAN absent from the input candidates.
**Tests to run:** new `testing.DescribeVerifierRegressionTest`; `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [src/chess/describe/ARCHITECTURE.md](src/chess/describe/ARCHITECTURE.md), [t5.md](wiki/t5.md).
**Labels:** `describe`, `grounding`, `P1`.

#### M4-2 ŌĆö "Why/plan" sentences from already-collected strategic tags
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** [PositionDescriptionExtractor.java](src/chess/describe/PositionDescriptionExtractor.java) collects KingSafety/Structure/passer tags but [ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java) never turns them into causation sentences ŌĆö the headline insight gap (self-scored ~4/10).
**Implementation notes:** Add deterministic causation phrasing in the classical generator keyed off existing tags (e.g. backward pawn ŌåÆ plan target). Keep faithful-by-construction: only assert what the input contains. No new model.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Positions with a clear structural feature produce a grounded "why/plan" sentence.
- [x] Output remains byte-deterministic (golden tests).
**Tests to run:** `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest` describe golden cases (add strategic/endgame/malformed-FEN coverage the TODO flags as missing); `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [src/chess/describe/ARCHITECTURE.md](src/chess/describe/ARCHITECTURE.md).
**Labels:** `describe`, `grounding`, `P1`.

#### M4-3 ŌĆö Unify the dual-T5 story; retire the dead describe-T5 stub
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** Two unrelated "T5" subsystems both surface as "T5": the working [Runner.java](src/chess/nn/t5/Runner.java) (behind `fen text`/`puzzle text`) and the permanent dead stub [T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java) (`available()==false` always). Users reasonably expect `position describe --engine t5` to reuse the working runtime; it does not.
**Implementation notes:** Either bridge `position describe --engine t5` onto `chess.nn.t5` (with the M4-1 verifier in front), or remove `--engine t5` from describe until weights exist and document the single T5 path. Prefer bridging if a position-prompt fits the existing tokenizer.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] No CLI surface advertises a T5 path that always throws "unavailable" without explanation.
- [x] Docs describe exactly one T5 runtime.
**Tests to run:** `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest`; `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [t5.md](wiki/t5.md), [glossary.md](wiki/glossary.md).
**Labels:** `describe`, `t5`, `cleanup`, `P2`.

---

### Milestone M5 ŌĆö Serve + SDK (theme E)

A **localhost-only analysis/automation daemon** ŌĆö explicitly NOT online play/matchmaking/cloud (hard product boundary). Depends on M1 catalog/schemas so the server exposes generated contracts, not hardcoded ones.

#### M5-1 ŌĆö Localhost JSON-RPC daemon over `application.Main`
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** No server exists (confirmed: no `ServerSocket`/`HttpServer` in src). Every CLI invocation pays JVM startup; interactive agents need a warm process.
**Implementation notes:** Use the JDK's built-in `com.sun.net.httpserver.HttpServer` (no third-party dep, satisfies the no-deps rule) bound to `127.0.0.1` only. Dispatch requests through the existing [Main.java](src/application/Main.java) command path; return JSON. Expose `crtk help --json` (M1-1) as a discovery endpoint. Default off; started via `crtk serve --port`.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] `crtk serve` binds localhost only and refuses non-loopback by default.
- [x] A request to run `fen validate` returns the same JSON the CLI emits.
- [x] No play/matchmaking/social endpoints.
**Tests to run:** new `testing.ServeRegressionTest` (loopback round-trip); `cli`.
**Docs to update:** new `wiki/serve.md`, [ai-agents.md](wiki/ai-agents.md).
**Labels:** `serve`, `agents`, `P2`.

#### M5-2 ŌĆö Generated Python SDK stub from the command catalog
**Priority:** P3
**Context:** No SDK; agents scrape prose. With M1-1 catalog + M5-1 daemon, a thin generated client is cheap and stays in sync.
**Implementation notes:** A generator (Python script under `scripts/`) reads `crtk help --json` and emits a typed Python client that calls the daemon. Keep generated, not hand-maintained, to avoid drift.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Regenerating the SDK from a changed catalog produces updated bindings without manual edits.
- [x] A smoke script runs `fen validate` through the SDK.
**Tests to run:** SDK smoke in `docs`/a new optional target (Python presence gated).
**Docs to update:** `wiki/serve.md`.
**Labels:** `sdk`, `agents`, `P3`.

---

Pause net-new UI expansion; let the Workbench mirror new CLI capabilities (PGN DB, review). Reuse the registry-driven [WindowLifecycle.java](src/application/gui/workbench/window/WindowLifecycle.java).

#### M6-1 ŌĆö Reconcile wiki/workbench.md with the 8-view shell

**Implementation notes:** Rewrite the tab map to the 8-view + modes structure (Board/Run/Engine Lab as switched surfaces).

**Docs to update:** [workbench.md](wiki/workbench.md), [workbench-design-guide.md](wiki/workbench-design-guide.md).

#### M6-2 ŌĆö Surface PGN DB + Review in the Workbench command palette
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** New CLI verbs (M2/M3) should appear in the palette automatically via the "All CLI" template, but curated templates and palette actions need entries.
**Implementation notes:** Add curated templates in [CommandTemplates.java](src/application/gui/workbench/command/CommandTemplates.java) for `pgn import/query` and `review game`; ensure `WorkbenchCommandRegression` still asserts full registry coverage.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] New verbs are reachable from the palette and the "All CLI" template resolves them.
**Tests to run:** `testing.WorkbenchCommandRegression` via `WorkbenchRegressionTest`.

#### M6-3 ŌĆö Split oversized Workbench files under the 2000-line cap headroom
**Priority:** P3
**Context:** 9 files exceed 2000 raw lines ([Theme.java], BoardPanel, WindowLifecycle, etc.); the structure regression passes only because comments are stripped. Little headroom.
**Implementation notes:** Extract cohesive helpers from the largest files; also add `engine`/`draw`/`play`/`relations` to `EXPECTED_FEATURE_PACKAGES` in [WorkbenchStructureRegressionTest.java](src/testing/WorkbenchStructureRegressionTest.java) so they get package-info/layout coverage.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] No file exceeds the cap after stripping; raw-line headroom restored on the top offenders.
- [x] Structure regression covers the previously-omitted subpackages.
**Progress:** `Theme.java`, `WindowLifecycle.java`, `BoardPanel.java`, `WindowBoardLayer.java`, `TreePanel.java`, `DrawPanel.java`, `PublishingPanel.java`, `EngineGauntletPanel.java`, and `MctsSearch.java` now have raw-line headroom via cohesive helper extraction; `DrawPanel.java` is at 1840 raw lines after the Draw color-format helper slice, `MctsSearch.java` is at 1696 raw lines after moving leaf scoring into `MctsSearchScorer`, and `TreePanel.java` is at 1692 raw lines after moving growth-history playback into `TreeScrubber`.
**Tests to run:** `testing.WorkbenchStructureRegressionTest`; `core`.
**Docs to update:** none.
**Labels:** `workbench`, `tech-debt`, `P3`.

### Milestone M7 ŌĆö Packaging & onboarding (theme J)

Fix cheap correctness bugs now; defer cross-platform bundles. Depends on M8 (checksums) for the model-fetch fix overlap.

#### M7-1 ŌĆö `doctor --json` and `config show --json`
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** [DoctorCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/DoctorCommand.java) and [ConfigCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/ConfigCommand.java) emit human lines only; only `version` has JSON. A daemon/editor (E/K) must scrape text.
**Implementation notes:** Add `--json` to both, emitting `{status, java, config, protocol, engineInstances, output, warnings[], errors[]}`. Extend doctor to also report native-lib presence (reuse [GpuCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/GpuCommand.java) backend matrix).
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] `crtk doctor --json` and `crtk config show --json` emit stable objects.
- [x] Exit codes unchanged (0/1/2).
**Tests to run:** `testing.CLICommandRegressionTest`; `cli` (passed).
**Docs to update:** [support.md](wiki/support.md), [troubleshooting.md](wiki/troubleshooting.md), [configuration.md](wiki/configuration.md) (updated).
**Labels:** `cli`, `packaging`, `agents`, `P2`.

#### M7-2 ŌĆö jpackage/jlink self-contained Linux runtime (groundwork)
**Priority:** P3
**Context:** Install is clone+`install.sh` (apt-only). A self-contained runtime lowers onboarding friction without changing the build to Maven/Gradle.
**Implementation notes:** Add a `scripts/make_runtime_linux.sh` using JDK `jlink`/`jpackage` over the existing `out/`+jar; keep `javac --release 17` as the compile step. Linux only in this issue; Win/macOS deferred.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] A produced bundle runs `crtk version` without a system JDK installed.
**Tests to run:** manual smoke (document in releasing.md); no harness target required. Passed with `scripts/make_runtime_linux.sh --version v1.0.0`, whose generated launcher runs `crtk version` with an empty `PATH`.
**Docs to update:** [releasing.md](wiki/releasing.md), [build-and-install.md](wiki/build-and-install.md) (updated).
**Labels:** `packaging`, `P3`.
