### Milestone M8 ŌĆö Dataset / ML provenance (theme I)

Make the "reproducible datasets" promise true. Depends on M1 (schemas) and the RunManifest provenance pattern.

#### M8-1 ŌĆö Uniform provenance stamp on every dataset exporter
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** [wiki/datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md) claims byte-exact determinism and per-export meta, but [RecordDatasetExporter.java](src/chess/io/RecordDatasetExporter.java) writes **no** meta.json, and lc0/classifier meta capture no crtk version/git commit/input checksums/weights hash/command line.
**Implementation notes:** Add a shared `Provenance` helper (crtk version from [VersionCommand.java], git commit via a build-time best-effort or `unknown`, SHA-256 of inputs/weights, command line) and stamp it into every exporter's manifest sidecar. Reuse the SHA-256 method pattern from [RunManifest.java](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java). Add a manifest sidecar to the npy exporter.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Every `record dataset` and `record export` (where a sidecar makes sense) writes a manifest sidecar with version + input/weights checksums + command line.
- [x] npy export gains a manifest sidecar.
- [x] A given manifest can be matched back to its producing inputs by checksum.
**Tests to run:** wire + extend `testing.RecordLC0ExporterRegressionTest`, `testing.RecordTrainingJSONLRegressionTest` (M0-4); `cli`/new `dataset` target.
**Docs to update:** [datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md).
**Labels:** `datasets`, `provenance`, `P1`.

#### M8-2 ŌĆö Byte-reproducibility regression for a dataset export
**Priority:** P1
**Context:** Determinism is asserted in prose but never tested (no test diffs two runs). Provenance is meaningless if outputs are not actually reproducible.
**Implementation notes:** Add a test that runs `record dataset classifier` (or npy) twice on a fixed input and asserts byte-identical tensors (provenance meta excluded from the byte-compare since it carries a command line/checksums). Exclude any timestamp from the byte-compared payload.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] Two runs produce byte-identical tensor files.
- [x] Test runs in CI.
**Tests to run:** new `testing.DatasetDeterminismRegressionTest`; `ci`.
**Docs to update:** [datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md), [quality-and-testing.md](wiki/quality-and-testing.md).
**Labels:** `datasets`, `determinism`, `testing`, `P1`.

#### M8-3 ŌĆö Verify model-weight checksums in install.sh
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** [install.sh](install.sh) fetches NNUE/LC0/BT4 weights with **no** sha256 check, while [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh) already supports `--sha256`. Silent corruption/MITM risk; weakens the ML provenance story.
**Implementation notes:** Add an expected-checksum table to install.sh's model-fetch step and verify after download (reuse the `verify_sha256` approach from `fetch_lc0_net.sh`). Converge the two fetch paths or at least the verification helper.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] install.sh aborts on a checksum mismatch for any fetched weight file.
- [x] Checksums are documented in [models/README.md](models/README.md).
**Tests to run:** `testing.InstallScriptRegressionTest` (extend if it can assert the checksum step); `core`.
**Docs to update:** [models/README.md](models/README.md), [build-and-install.md](wiki/build-and-install.md).
**Labels:** `packaging`, `provenance`, `security`, `P2`.

#### M8-4 ŌĆö Train/val/test split for record datasets
**Priority:** P2
**Context:** No split exists anywhere (the only `--split` is GPU perft, unrelated). `record files --max-records` only shards by count; an ML toolkit needs holdout/group-aware splits.
**Implementation notes:** Add `--split train:val:test` (seeded, deterministic) and `--group-by` (e.g. by game/sister-group to prevent leakage) to the dataset/files commands in [RecordCommands.java](src/application/cli/command/RecordCommands.java). Write a manifest listing the split parts.
**Acceptance criteria:**
- [x] A seeded split is reproducible and leakage-free for group-aware mode.
- [x] A manifest indexes the produced parts.
**Tests to run:** `testing.RecordSplitRegressionTest`; `cli`.
**Docs to update:** [datasets.md](wiki/datasets.md).
**Labels:** `datasets`, `ml`, `P2`.

---

### Explicitly rejected / deferred (not issued)

Per the theme map, these get **no** issues:
- **L (plugins):** explicitly a NON-GOAL ([TODO.txt] line ~632); fights determinism/no-deps. The legitimate "add an engine" need is already met by TOML protocol config ([Protocol.java](src/chess/uci/Protocol.java)).
- **N (OTB/broadcast):** out of product boundary (pulls toward live/online), xlarge effort for an orthogonal audience.
- **O (OCR/scan):** requires a CV model incompatible with no-deps; belongs in the external playground, with CRTK consuming its PGN/FEN output via M2.
- **B beyond folder import:** account linking / continuous sync / social are forbidden by the product boundary; only the read-only file/folder slice (M2-2) is in scope.

---

These plans assume one primary maintainer working at the cadence implied by the recent commit history (feature-sized commits, not full-time team velocity). Estimates are deliberately conservative: every initiative below names a specific theme from the theme map (A, C, F, G, I, M, etc.) or a concrete file, and respects the preserved values (one shared core, plain `javac --release 17`, deterministic outputs, CLI-is-source-of-truth, no online-play boundary).

The ordering is driven by one structural fact established in the theme map and fact-check: **the existing roadmap ([TODO.txt](TODO.txt)) is an inward-facing polish backlog that never mentions the product foundations the stated goal requires** (local PGN database, game-review-to-study routing, machine-readable schemas, dataset provenance). Worse, it is partly stale ŌĆö it instructs contributors to rebuild [Threats.java](src/chess/tag/Threats.java) "from this spec" while that file is already a real 278-line implementation wired into [Generator.java](src/chess/tag/Generator.java) (`addStructuralThreats`, line 920). So the first move is cheap reconciliation (Theme M), then the schema substrate (Theme F) that everything else stands on.

---

## 17. 30-day plan ŌĆö what ships first

**Strategic intent for the month:** stop digging the polish hole, lay the contract substrate, and produce one demo that proves CRTK can do something it cannot do today: take a user's own PGN, and answer questions about it from the command line through a *stable, machine-readable contract*. Nothing in this month requires a trained model, a GPU, or a server ŌĆö all deferred deliberately (see Themes G, E, K verdicts: dependent on F).

#### What is explicitly POSTPONED this month (and why)
- **Theme E (local API server/SDK)** ŌĆö depends on F's command catalog existing first; building it now hard-codes contracts F would replace. Fact-check confirmed no server exists today (`ServerSocket`/`HttpServer` grep empty), so there is nothing to maintain in the interim.
- **Theme G generative T5 explanations** ŌĆö blocked on weights that do not exist. [T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java) `available()` returns `false` unconditionally and `generate()` throws. The *classical* describe path is already shipped and grounded; only its deepening is in scope later (Theme G is build-later/P1).
- **OTIS CUDA kernel optimization, MCTS graph canvas, NN view polish** ŌĆö TOO-INTERNAL per the TODO analysis. The naive OTIS CUDA backend already exists and works ([libotis_cuda.so](native/cuda/build/) is built); optimizing throughput of a network whose only shipped weights are a *random placeholder* ([Model.java](src/chess/nn/otis/Model.java), `DEFAULT_WEIGHTS=models/otis_policy_wdl_random.bin`) is premature.

#### Week 1 ŌĆö Reconcile the roadmap, close the landmine, fix the cheap correctness bugs
*Theme M (P1, small) + correctness items surfaced by the fact-check.*

- Reconcile [TODO.txt](TODO.txt) against HEAD: strike the three stale blocks (Threats "11-byte stub"; OTIS CUDA framed as greenfield "add an implementation"; interleaved `[DONE]` items mixed with open ones). Add the genuinely-absent product themes (A, C, F) as first-class roadmap entries. ~half a day; prevents a contributor redoing finished work.
- Close the [URGENT.md](URGENT.md) open checkbox: re-export or formally retire any pre-2026-06-02 OTIS weights (the channel-10 `pawn_attack_forward_oriented` direction bug), then delete the file or convert it to a tracked issue. Low blast radius today (only a random placeholder ships) but it is a silent geometric-correctness landmine the moment real OTIS weights appear.
- Fix [classifier Model.java](src/chess/nn/classifier/Model.java) `DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` path drift: it points at `models/classifier_...bin` but the shipped file is `models/puzzle-classifier_...bin`, so `loadDefault()` is broken out of the box (Theme I item, but it is a one-line fix).
- Fix the [getting-started.md](wiki/getting-started.md) doc-drift: it claims "a prebuilt `crtk.jar` ships in the repository root", but `crtk.jar` is gitignored ([.gitignore](.gitignore) line 31) ŌĆö a clean clone has no jar and the documented `java -jar crtk.jar version` fails. Either commit a build step into the quickstart or remove the false promise.
- Single-source the version: [VersionCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/VersionCommand.java) `VERSION="1.0.0"` and [package.json](package.json) `version` duplicate the literal with no enforcement. Add a regression assertion that they agree (cheap; prevents the "bug nobody notices" releasing.md itself warns about).

*Exit criteria:* roadmap matches reality, no stale rebuild instructions, the two correctness one-liners merged, version drift gated by a test.

#### Week 2 ŌĆö Machine-readable command catalog
*Theme F (P0, medium) ŌĆö part 1.*

- Serialize [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) to a `crtk help --json` (or `crtk schema commands`) output: areas, actions, aliases, summaries, usage tails, and exit-code conventions. The metadata **already lives in memory** on every [CliCommand](src/application/cli/CliCommand.java) node (`commandPath`, `aliasPaths`, `isRunnable`); this is serialization, not new modeling.
- Keep it in the noun-verb grammar and reuse the existing OutputMode plumbing in [CommandSupport.java](src/application/cli/command/CommandSupport.java) (`resolveOutputMode`, which already rejects `--json`+`--jsonl`).
- Add a regression in [CLICommandRegressionTest.java](src/testing/CLICommandRegressionTest.java) asserting the catalog covers every runnable leaf, mirroring the existing [WorkbenchCommandRegression](src/testing/WorkbenchCommandRegression.java) `testCommandControllerCoversCliRegistry` discipline.

*Exit criteria:* `crtk help --json` emits a stable catalog of the entire CLI tree; an agent can introspect capabilities without scraping prose.

#### Week 3 ŌĆö Stable record schema + fail-loud validation
*Theme F (P0, medium) ŌĆö part 2; sets up Theme A and I.*

- Add a `schemaVersion` field to [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) (currently a fixed 7-field shape with no version ŌĆö confirmed by fact-check). Bump tolerant parsing to read records missing the field as v1.
- Publish JSON Schema files for the load-bearing contracts: `.record`, `training-jsonl`, the dataset `meta.json` shapes, and the per-command JSON output shapes. These are *artifacts in the repo*, not runtime deps ŌĆö consistent with no-third-party-deps.
- Add a strict streaming mode to [RecordIO.java](src/application/cli/RecordIO.java): today `Record.fromJson`/`Reader` silently drop malformed input (fact-check confirmed). A `--strict` flag (or a `crtk record validate`) that fails loudly with the offending line is required for reproducible datasets.

*Exit criteria:* records carry a version; bad input fails loudly on demand; downstream tools (and the upcoming SDK) have schemas to validate against.

#### Week 4 ŌĆö First demo build + provenance stamping groundwork
*Theme I (P1, medium) ŌĆö the cheap, high-ROI half; plus demo assembly.*

- Add a uniform provenance stamp to every dataset exporter: crtk version, git commit (read at build time or via `git rev-parse` fallback), input file SHA-256, weights SHA-256 where applicable, and the command line. Reuse the existing [RunManifest.java](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java) SHA-256 pattern (`schema = "crtk.workbench.run-manifest.v1"`, per-file `sha256`). Critically: [RecordDatasetExporter.java](src/chess/io/RecordDatasetExporter.java) writes **no** `meta.json` at all today ŌĆö add one.
- Converge [install.sh](install.sh) model fetch onto the sha256-verifying path already in [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh) (`verify_sha256`). The installer currently downloads weights with no checksum (fact-check confirmed) ŌĆö a provenance and supply-chain gap.

#### THE FIRST DEMO (end of Week 4)

> **Demo: "Introspect and validate, end to end, with a contract."**
>
> 1. `crtk help --json | jq '.areas[].actions | length'` ŌĆö show the entire CLI surface is now machine-readable.
> 2. Pipe a deliberately-malformed `.record` file through `crtk record validate` (or `--strict`) and watch it fail loudly with the exact offending line ŌĆö contrast with today's silent drop.
> 3. Run `crtk record dataset npy -i puzzles.record -o demo` and `cat demo.meta.json` ŌĆö show it now carries crtk version, git commit, input checksum, and command line, where four weeks ago it produced *no* meta file.
> 4. `crtk version --json` and the new schema files validate against the actual output.

This demo is small, but it is honest and it is the *foundation* every later theme depends on. It proves the toolkit is now self-describing and reproducible ŌĆö the precondition the theme map flags as gating E, K, A, C, and I. It deliberately does **not** promise a PGN database or explanations yet; over-promising those in month one would mean shipping unstable contracts.

---

## 18. 90-day plan ŌĆö milestones + demos

By end of quarter the headline is: **CRTK can ingest, store, query, and review a user's own games from the CLI**, with the workbench mirroring it for free. This is the single biggest gap toward "best local-first study toolkit" (Theme A, build-now/P1) and its dependent reviewer (Theme C, build-now/P1).

#### Milestone 1 (Ōēł weeks 5ŌĆō9) ŌĆö Local PGN database (`crtk pgn`)
*Theme A (P1, large). Depends on F (done in the 30-day plan).*

- Promote the in-memory logic from [PgnExplorerModel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) (index/filter/dedupe ŌĆö currently workbench-only, no CLI peer, confirmed) into the `chess.*` core so CLI and workbench share one implementation, preserving the one-shared-core invariant.
- Add a noun-verb `crtk pgn` area: `import`, `index`, `query`, `show`, `stats`. Backed by a local JSONL/`.record`-style store keyed on a game id + position `signatureCore()` ([Position.java](src/chess/core/Position.java), the FNV-1a digest ŌĆö *not* a Zobrist key; document the collision policy for large stores as an ASSUMPTION to validate).
- Extend [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) with game-id and provenance fields (event/players/date/move-number) ŌĆö today `training-jsonl` hard-codes `game_id:null`. Reuse [Pgn.java](src/chess/struct/Pgn.java)/[Game.java](src/chess/struct/Game.java) for parse/round-trip and [Converter.java](src/chess/io/Converter.java) for recordŌåöPGN linking.
- **Boundary note:** this is strictly local files. No online import yet (Theme B is deferred/P3, boundary-gated to read-only file import only).

**Demo (week 9):** `crtk pgn import my-games.pgn`, then `crtk pgn query --result loss --opening "Sicilian"` returns indexed games; `crtk pgn show <game-id> --json` round-trips through the shared core; the workbench [PgnExplorerModel](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) now reads the same on-disk store.

#### Milestone 2 (Ōēł weeks 10ŌĆō13) ŌĆö Game-review-to-study router (`crtk review`)
*Theme C (P1, large). Depends on A (store) and F (study-unit schema).*

- A CLI verb that ingests a stored game, detects blunders/turning-points, and emits study units (puzzle Records for the refutation + annotated lines). The grounded primitives all exist: [GameAnalyzer.java](src/chess/tag/game/GameAnalyzer.java)/[LineAnalyzer.java](src/chess/tag/game/LineAnalyzer.java)/[VariationAnalyzer.java](src/chess/tag/game/VariationAnalyzer.java) (real impls, ~1007 lines), [RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand.java) (eval-drift signal), and external grading via [Engine.java](src/chess/uci/Engine.java) + [Pool.java](src/application/Pool.java).
- **Prerequisite that must land inside this milestone:** register the dynamic tag families `MOVE_EFFECT`/`LINE`/`VARIATION`/`GAME` in [Sort.java](src/chess/tag/Sort.java) `FAMILY_ORDER` and [Literals.java](src/chess/tag/core/Literals.java), and document them in [SCHEMA.md](tag/SCHEMA.md). Today they bypass the canonical sort/dedupe/Filter pipeline via inline string literals (e.g. [MoveEffect.java](src/chess/tag/MoveEffect.java) `PREFIX = "MOVE_EFFECT: san="`) ŌĆö confirmed by fact-check. The reviewer cannot reliably consume them until they are first-class.
- The engine-graded `quality=`/`turning_point` verdicts the digest flags as deferred must route through external UCI for reference-grade grading (the in-house path is not reference-grade by design; preserved value).
- Wrap the refutation into a puzzle Record using existing [MineCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/MineCommand.java) machinery ŌĆö this is the "the human played X, the puzzle is the refutation" pipeline mining explicitly does *not* do today.

**Demo (week 13):** `crtk review <game-id> --output study/` produces, from a real lost game, (a) a turning-point report, (b) puzzle Records for the missed refutations, (c) annotated mainline tags ŌĆö all deterministic and grounded.

#### Milestone 3 (Ōēł weeks 10ŌĆō13, parallel) ŌĆö Quality stream + describe deepening groundwork
*Theme G groundwork (P1, build-later) + capped Theme 1 hygiene from TODO analysis.*

- Classical `position describe` fact-ranking improvements and the missing golden tests the TODO itself flags (tactical/strategic/quiet/endgame/malformed-FEN) on [ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/ClassicalPositionDescriptionGenerator.java). The structured input already *collects* `KingSafety`/`Structure`/passer tags in [PositionDescriptionExtractor.java](src/chess/describe/PositionDescriptionExtractor.java) but never turns them into "why/plan" sentences ŌĆö begin closing that gap.
- Run SonarLint hygiene as a **capped background stream** (TODO Theme 1), explicitly not gating the product milestones above.
- Fix the live-NN-visualization regression (start/end-only frames) ŌĆö a real bug ŌĆö without building the demoted graph canvas.

#### End-of-quarter state (what is working)
- `crtk pgn` stores, indexes, and queries the user's own games locally.
- `crtk review` turns a game into grounded study units.
- Every dataset export carries provenance; bad input fails loudly; the whole CLI is machine-readable via `crtk help --json` with published JSON Schemas.
- The dynamic tag families are canonical and documented.
- The workbench mirrors the new CLI verbs for free (CLI-is-source-of-truth holds).

**ASSUMPTION:** Milestones 1 and 2 are each ~4ŌĆō5 weeks for a single maintainer. If A slips, C slips with it (hard dependency on the store). The realistic risk is A's on-disk store format design; mitigate by reusing the existing tolerant [Reader.java](src/chess/io/Reader.java)/[Writer.java](src/chess/io/Writer.java) append-safe JSON-array machinery rather than inventing a new container.

---

## 19. 6ŌĆō12 month plan ŌĆö the bigger vision after foundations

With a local game database, a review router, stable schemas, and provenance in place, the second half of the year turns CRTK from "a deterministic chess toolbox" into "the local-first study and research workbench" ŌĆö without crossing the hard product boundary (no online play, matchmaking, social, anti-cheat, or cloud-credit platform; no chasing Stockfish strength).

#### Initiative 1 (months 4ŌĆō6) ŌĆö Local analysis daemon + SDKs
*Theme E (P2, large). Depends on F (now done).*

- A **localhost-only** JSON-RPC/HTTP daemon fronting [Main.java](src/application/Main.java), exposing the F command catalog and the in-process engine APIs ([AlphaBeta.java](src/chess/engine/AlphaBeta.java), [Mcts.java](src/chess/engine/Mcts.java), [MateProver.java](src/chess/engine/MateProver.java), [See.java](src/chess/eval/See.java)) plus the streaming hook that already exists ([Engine.java](src/chess/uci/Engine.java) `analyseInfinite`/`onUpdate`).
- **Boundary discipline (load-bearing):** this is an analysis/automation daemon bound to localhost only. It MUST NOT acquire matchmaking, account, or cloud-credit surface. Every endpoint maps 1:1 to an existing CLI verb; no online-play primitives.
- Generate Python/TS SDK stubs *from* the F catalog so they cannot drift. Solves the per-invocation JVM-startup cost that makes interactive agent use slow today (every `crtk` call pays cold-start).

#### Initiative 2 (months 5ŌĆō7) ŌĆö VSCode/Jupyter integration
*Theme K (P2, medium, deferred until E). Builds on F + E.*

- VSCode tasks/completion driven by `crtk help --json`; a thin Jupyter wrapper over the daemon so notebook cells avoid JVM cold-start. The `.npy` exports already make it notebook-friendly; the daemon makes it interactive. Parasitic on F/E by design ŌĆö no value attempting it before them.

#### Initiative 3 (months 6ŌĆō9) ŌĆö Repertoire / SRS, explanation-first
*Theme D (P2, large). Depends on A, C, F, G.*

- A spaced-repetition layer that schedules review items produced by `crtk review` (Theme C) and opening lines from the bundled 3,412-entry complete A00-E99 ECO book ([Encyclopedia.java](src/chess/eco/Encyclopedia.java)).
- **Prerequisite:** promote the CLI-local `eco continuations` logic into a reusable `chess.eco` opening-tree/line-continuation API before repertoire matching depends on it. Also note [Encyclopedia.java](src/chess/eco/Encyclopedia.java) reaches `Toml.tableArrays` via reflection ŌĆö brittle; harden before building an SDK/export contract on top.
- Card state and scheduling persist as versioned Records (the `schemaVersion` field from Theme F earns its keep here). Identity keyed on `signatureCore()`.
- Keep `crtk eco lookup/search/continuations/validate` as the user-facing surface, and move any repertoire-needed tree traversal into the shared ECO package rather than duplicating CLI code.

#### Initiative 4 (months 7ŌĆō10) ŌĆö Grounded generative explanations
*Theme G deepening (P1, build-later). Depends on C for whole-game context.*

- Wire the *working* tag-to-text path ([Runner.java](src/chess/nn/t5/Runner.java) + [TagPrompt.java](src/chess/nn/t5/TagPrompt.java), "do not invent moves") into `position describe`, replacing the dead [T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java) stub. Resolve the confusing dual-T5 story (two unrelated "T5" subsystems both surfaced as `--engine t5`).
- **Implement the inference-time grounding/verification pass** documented in [ARCHITECTURE.md](src/chess/describe/ARCHITECTURE.md) but never coded: every SAN the model names must be a legal candidate; on contradiction, fall back to the faithful classical text. This must exist *before* any generative weights are wired in ŌĆö it is the hallucination guard.
- Training-data export (the deterministic classical text as the faithfulness floor) feeds an external trainer (the separate playground repo); CRTK stays no-deps and inference-only. **ASSUMPTION:** trained position-description weights remain out of scope unless the external pipeline produces them; the classical+verification path delivers value regardless.

#### Initiative 5 (months 8ŌĆō12) ŌĆö Provenance-grade datasets + reproducibility gate
*Theme I deepening + Theme M discipline.*

- Dataset manifests tying multi-shard exports into one signed bundle; a reproducibility regression that asserts byte-equality across two runs (today the wiki *claims* byte-exact determinism but no test verifies it, and [Result.java](src/chess/engine/Result.java) `equals()` includes `elapsedMillis`, a documented CI foot-gun). Add a time-stripped "deterministic record" comparison.
- Wire the six currently-orphaned ML/dataset tests ([RecordTrainingJSONLRegressionTest](src/testing/RecordTrainingJSONLRegressionTest.java), [RecordLC0ExporterRegressionTest](src/testing/RecordLC0ExporterRegressionTest.java), NNUE, Upstream, PlayMode, Booleans) into [run_regression_suite.sh](scripts/run_regression_suite.sh) ŌĆö they compile but never gate CI (fact-check confirmed), so the ML pillar is unguarded.

#### Explicitly out of scope for the year (REJECTED themes, restated to prevent scope creep)
- **Theme L (plugins):** rejected in-repo ([TODO.txt](TODO.txt):632 "NON-GOAL: a plugin framework"). The legitimate extension need ŌĆö adding a UCI engine ŌĆö is already met by config-as-extension via [Protocol.java](src/chess/uci/Protocol.java) TOML. A plugin system fights determinism and the no-deps build.
- **Theme N (OTB/broadcast)** and **Theme O (OCR/scan):** rejected. Both pull toward live/online I/O or require a CV model incompatible with the no-third-party-deps constraint. If ever pursued, OCR belongs in the external playground and reduces to "import a PGN" via Theme A.
- **Theme B (platform sync):** deferred/P3, and only ever as read-only file/public-export import folded into `crtk pgn import`. Account linking / continuous sync / matchmaking are forbidden by the product boundary.
- **Theme H (workbench expansion):** the workbench is already the most-developed surface; net-new UI expansion is paused. It benefits *for free* as A/C/F/G land (its [PgnExplorerModel](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java)/[GameReviewPanel](src/application/gui/workbench/game/GameReviewPanel.java) become real productized surfaces). Address the 2000-line-file and stale-doc debt opportunistically, not as a milestone.

#### Where CRTK stands at 12 months
A local-first toolkit that stores your games, reviews them into grounded study units and spaced-repetition cards, explains positions without hallucinating, exports provenance-stamped reproducible ML datasets, and exposes all of it through a self-describing CLI, a localhost SDK, and editor/notebook integration ŌĆö built on one shared chess core with plain `javac`, no third-party Java deps, and no step toward an online-play platform.

---

## 20. Risk register

This register tracks the risks that the proposed roadmap (themes F, A, C, I, M build-now; G, H, J, E, D build-later; B/K deferred; L/N/O rejected) introduces or fails to retire. Likelihood and Impact are rated against the project as it exists today, not an idealized version. Every entry is grounded in a specific file, contract, or fact-check finding; assumptions are marked **ASSUMPTION**.

The dominant theme across this register: CRTK's value is its *preserved invariants* (one shared core, deterministic outputs, plain `javac --release 17`, stable JSON contracts, grounded explanations, hard product boundary). Most serious risks are not "feature X is hard" ŌĆö they are "feature X quietly erodes an invariant." The mitigations are therefore mostly about *gating* changes behind tests and schemas rather than about adding capability.

### Risk table

| # | Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------------|
| 1 | **Scope creep toward online play / matchmaking / social.** The roadmap adds a PGN store (A), a review router (C), and "build-later" a localhost API server (E). Each is one step from the forbidden boundary (online play, anti-cheat, cloud credit). Theme B (platform import) sits *on* the line. | M | H | Treat the HARD product boundary as a CI-enforceable invariant, not a guideline. E is localhost-only analysis/automation; B is read-only ingestion of user-supplied PGN/public exports ŌĆö no account linking, no continuous sync, no matchmaking. Add a written "boundary test" checklist to [AGENTS.md](AGENTS.md) that every new area must pass. Reject L/N/O as already decided ([TODO.txt](TODO.txt):632 "NON-GOAL: a plugin framework"). |
| 2 | **Losing deterministic output contracts.** Determinism is the headline value (`AGENTS.md`: "same input produces the same output every time") but it is enforced by *convention*, not tests. [Result.java](src/chess/engine/Result.java) `equals()` includes `elapsedMillis` (line 106) ŌĆö a known foot-gun; `puzzle-elo-jsonl` runs multi-threaded tree search with no reproducibility test; mining dir-mode bakes `System.currentTimeMillis()` into filenames. New stores/routers add more wall-clock and threading. | H | H | Add a determinism regression that runs representative commands twice and `diff`s (the wiki documents the manual version; automate it). For new exporters, strip runtime fields (time/nps) from any field that participates in golden comparison. Forbid `System.currentTimeMillis()`/`Random` without a fixed seed in any path that writes a dataset/store row. |
| 3 | **Schema drift across three+ descriptions of the surface.** Today the command surface lives in [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java), an 83KB embedded [HelpCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/HelpCommand.java), and a 69KB `wiki/command-reference.md`, kept in sync by hand. Theme F adds a `crtk help --json` catalog + JSON Schema files ŌĆö a *fourth* source that can drift. | H | M | Make F's `--json` catalog *generated from* `CliRegistry` (the metadata already lives in memory), not hand-authored. Generate `command-reference.md` from the same model. Add a regression that fails if the catalog and registry disagree (the pattern exists: [WorkbenchCommandRegression.java](src/testing/WorkbenchCommandRegression.java) already walks `CliRegistry.root()`). |
| 4 | **Record schema has no version field ŌĆö silent format evolution.** [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) is a fixed 7-field shape with NO `schemaVersion` (fact-check confirmed). A (PGN store) and C (study units) must extend it; without versioning, old `.record` files become ambiguous and `fromJson` "tolerant parsing" drops unknown shapes silently. | H | H | F must add `schemaVersion` to `Record` *before* A/C extend it. Publish a JSON Schema per version. Add a strict-mode reader path in [RecordIO.java](src/application/cli/RecordIO.java) that fails loudly on unknown/malformed rows instead of the current silent skip, so format drift is detectable. |
| 5 | **Silent data loss from tolerant parsing.** `Record.fromJson` and `Reader.*` return null / skip on malformed input with no error channel (digest + [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) comment "tolerant parsing for this fixed shape"). `exportFromRatingCsv` silently drops rows with <22 fields. A corrupt dump yields a quietly-smaller dataset ŌĆö fatal for "reproducible datasets." | M | H | Add an opt-in strict mode and a per-line error report to the streaming readers. Default exporters to print a one-line `skipped: N (reasons)` summary to stderr (some already count internally ŌĆö surface it). This is cheap and pairs with F. |
| 6 | **UI complexity / Workbench overdevelopment crowds out product work.** H is already the most-funded theme (8-view shell, 5 TODO sub-themes). Nine workbench files exceed 2000 raw lines ([Theme.java](src/application/gui/workbench/window/Theme.java) 3076, `BoardPanel` 2763, etc.); the 2000-line cap passes only because comments are stripped. Continuing UI polish at P0/P1 starves A/C/F. | H | M | Demote H to build-later/P2 per the theme map; freeze net-new top-level UI surfaces until A/C land. Let the workbench *mirror* new CLI verbs (it auto-picks them up via [CommandTemplates.java](src/application/gui/workbench/command/CommandTemplates.java)). Address the file-size/coverage debt opportunistically, not as a gate. |
| 7 | **Workbench becomes a second implementation of core logic.** The CLI-is-source-of-truth invariant holds today because the workbench shells out via [CommandRunner.java](src/application/gui/workbench/command/CommandRunner.java) (fact-check confirmed: spawns `application.Main` child JVM). But Board/Play/Relations already run *in-process* through `chess.core`, and A's plan is to promote `PgnExplorerModel` (in-memory, workbench-only) into core. If review/store logic is written in the GUI first, it forks. | M | H | Promote `PgnExplorerModel`/`GameReviewPanel` logic *into* `chess.*` core and have BOTH the CLI and workbench call it ŌĆö never the reverse. Keep `WorkbenchCommandRegression.testCommandControllerCoversCliRegistry` green so any GUI-only command path is caught. |
| 8 | **Packaging burden balloons (cross-platform).** J is Ubuntu/apt-only ([install.sh](install.sh):5 "crtk installer (Ubuntu)"), the only release packager is CUDA-only ([make_release_linux_cuda.sh](scripts/make_release_linux_cuda.sh)). Supporting Windows/macOS bundles + jpackage/jlink is broad effort that does not advance the study mission. | M | M | Keep cross-platform packaging at P2/build-later. The portable jar runs anywhere Java 17 does ŌĆö document that path. Fix the *cheap* correctness bugs now (see #9, #20). Do not commit to MSI/dmg/Homebrew until A/C/F ship. |
| 9 | **Onboarding doc-drift breaks first run.** [getting-started.md](wiki/getting-started.md):48 claims "a prebuilt `crtk.jar` ships in the repository root" but `crtk.jar` is gitignored ([.gitignore](.gitignore):31) ŌĆö fact-check confirmed a clean clone has no jar, so `java -jar crtk.jar version` fails immediately. `wiki/workbench.md` still documents 12 tabs vs the shipped 6/8. | H | M | Fold into M (roadmap reconciliation) + the Documentation Site theme ŌĆö both cheap and bounded. Fix the jar claim, regenerate the workbench tab docs from reality. Add a docs link/claim smoke check to the `docs` CI target. |
| 10 | **API/SDK maintenance treadmill (E).** A localhost server + Python + TS SDKs is large and must stay in sync with the command surface forever. Building it before F means hard-coding contracts F would replace. | M | M | Gate E behind F: the server fronts `application.Main` and exposes F's *generated* catalog/schemas; SDK stubs are *generated* from the catalog, not hand-written. Defer to P2. Reuse the existing streaming hook [Engine.java](src/chess/uci/Engine.java) `analyseInfinite`/`onUpdate` rather than inventing a new one. |
| 11 | **Platform import fragility (B).** Lichess/Chess.com APIs change, rate-limit, and add ToS constraints; even read-only fetch adds a network dependency to a deterministic, offline-first tool and edges toward the boundary. | M | M | Scope B strictly to read-only ingestion of *user-supplied* PGN/export files first ("folder import" is just a subset of A's `pgn import`). Treat any network fetcher as P3, optional, and isolated behind a clear seam so the core never depends on it. Never persist credentials. |
| 12 | **Hallucinated explanations once a generative model is wired in.** G's deterministic path is faithful-by-construction today, but the describe-T5 is a permanent stub ([T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java): `available()==false`, `generate()` throws ŌĆö fact-check confirmed) and the documented inference-time grounding/verification pass (legal-SAN check, fallback-to-classical) is *unimplemented*. The day a T5 lands, hallucination protection does not exist in code. | M | H | Implement the grounding/verification pass ([ARCHITECTURE.md](src/chess/describe/ARCHITECTURE.md) describes it) BEFORE wiring any generative weights: every SAN the model names must be a legal candidate; on contradiction, fall back to the classical text. Keep the classical generator as the faithfulness anchor. Gate G-generative behind C (so it has grounded game context) and behind this pass. |
| 13 | **Confusing dual-T5 story misleads users and duplicates effort.** Two unrelated subsystems both surface as "T5": the working [Runner.java](src/chess/nn/t5/Runner.java) (behind `fen text`/`puzzle text`) and the dead [T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java](src/chess/describe/T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java) stub (behind `position describe --engine t5`). A user expects `--engine t5` to reuse the working runtime; it does not. | M | M | When deepening G, bridge `position describe --engine t5` to the working `chess.nn.t5` runtime instead of reviving the dead stub. Document the one T5 path. Until then, keep the "unavailable" message explicit (it already is) so no fake output is presented. |
| 14 | **Local PGN database performance / store design.** A keys games on `Position.signatureCore()`, which is a 64-bit **FNV-1a digest, not a Zobrist hash** (fact-check confirmed via [Position.java](src/chess/core/Position.java)). It is "fast cache key" grade with an *undocumented collision policy*; at library scale (millions of positions) collisions and repeated FEN re-parse (`Record.fromJson -> new Position(fen)`) become real. The single-writer seek-rewrite in `Writer.appendJsonObjects` is not concurrency-safe. | M | H | For A, document the collision policy explicitly and store the full FEN alongside the signature so lookups verify on FEN equality (the ECO loader already does exact + signature lookup in [Encyclopedia.java](src/chess/eco/Encyclopedia.java)). Use an append-safe JSONL store with a side index rather than the trailing-bracket rewrite for concurrent writes. Benchmark at 100k+ games before declaring A done. |
| 15 | **Java dependency creep.** The no-third-party-deps / plain-javac invariant is a core differentiator (fact-check: no pom/gradle, no non-JDK imports). A PGN DB tempts SQLite/H2; an API server tempts Jetty/Netty; SDKs tempt JSON libs. | M | H | Hold the line: A uses the existing hand-rolled JSON ([utility.Json]) + JSONL files, not an embedded SQL engine. E uses `com.sun.net.httpserver` (JDK built-in) not a framework. Add `SourceHeaderRegressionTest`-style import bans for new third-party packages so a stray `import org.*`/`import com.*` fails CI. |
| 16 | **Cross-platform behavior divergence in deterministic outputs.** PDF rendering depends on installed AWT fonts and a hardcoded `/usr/share/texmf/...` Latin Modern path ([Font.java](src/chess/pdf/document/Font.java):91), and `Document.escape()` maps non-ASCII to `?` ([Document.java](src/chess/pdf/document/Document.java):230). The same manifest yields different bytes / wraps on a machine without TeX, contradicting the "byte-stable, diffable in VCS" claim. | M | M | Document the font dependency as a known non-portability. **ASSUMPTION:** bundling a single open font (or embedding metrics) would restore byte-stability but adds a binary asset ŌĆö defer unless publishing becomes a priority. For now, scope determinism claims to "same machine, same fonts" and say so in `wiki/book-publishing.md`. |
| 17 | **Test suite slowness / single-job CI stalls.** CI is one `ubuntu-latest` job, sequential `main()`-per-test, no timeout, no matrix ([ci.yml](.github/workflows/ci.yml)). A hung UCI handshake or Workbench Robot path blocks the gate indefinitely. A (store) and C (router) add heavier end-to-end tests. | M | M | Add per-step timeouts to the CI job. Keep new A/C regressions bounded (small fixture corpora). Wire the six currently-unwired ML tests (#21) into a non-blocking nightly rather than the push gate if they are slow. |
| 18 | **Native GPU complexity (CUDA/ROCm/oneAPI) maintenance.** Parity is maintained by hand-keeping `native/common/*.inl` byte-identical to the Java forward passes (e.g. [otis_gpu_impl.inl](native/common/otis_gpu_impl.inl) mirrors `Model.java`). Any change must be mirrored in two languages or parity silently breaks. CI never builds or exercises native backends; parity tests self-skip without hardware. | M | M | Treat GPU as optional and frozen unless explicitly funded; demote OTIS CUDA *kernel optimization* (TODO theme 5) ŌĆö the lib already exists and works (fact-check). Keep the one real correctness item (policy parity, #22). **ASSUMPTION:** a host-emulated parity test in CI would close the "self-skip" gap but is non-trivial ŌĆö defer. |
| 19 | **Model artifact management is ad hoc and unverified.** Weights are fetched by [install.sh](install.sh) from hardcoded URLs with **no sha256 verification** (fact-check confirmed; [fetch_lc0_net.sh](scripts/fetch_lc0_net.sh) supports `--sha256`, install.sh does not). Supply-chain + corruption risk; no `crtk model` management, no manifest, no checksum pinning. The classifier `loadDefault()` is **broken** against the shipped tree (`DEFAULT_WEIGHTS=models/classifier_...` vs shipped `puzzle-classifier_...`). | M | H | Fold into I: converge install.sh onto the sha256-verifying fetch path; pin checksums in a manifest. Fix the classifier `DEFAULT_WEIGHTS` path drift ([Model.java](src/chess/nn/classifier/Model.java)) ŌĆö it is a one-line bug that breaks the one model with a clear ML story. |
| 20 | **User confusion from documented-vs-actual defaults.** `engine builtin` *actually* defaults to NNUE-if-installed ([BuiltInEngineCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/BuiltInEngineCommand.java):580, fact-check confirmed) while `wiki/in-house-engine.md` says "default is classical." Version is duplicated in [VersionCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/VersionCommand.java):20 and `package.json` with no enforcement. Reproducibility-by-documentation fails when docs lie. | M | M | Fix in M: reconcile the default-evaluator doc with code (or change the code to match the doc ŌĆö pick one and test it). Single-source the version (inject from git tag or assert agreement in a test). Cheap, removes a recurring "why did my result change" support load. |
| 21 | **Stale roadmap causes redone/finished work.** [TODO.txt](TODO.txt) tells contributors to rebuild [Threats.java](src/chess/tag/Threats.java) "from this spec" because it is "an 11-byte stub" ŌĆö fact-check confirmed it is a real ~278-line/10.6KB impl already wired into `Generator`. OTIS CUDA is framed as greenfield though the lib is built. Six ML tests exist but are unwired from CI (fact-check). A reader trusting the TODO wastes days. | H | M | Run M (reconciliation) FIRST: strike the three stale blocks, mark shipped items DONE, wire (or nightly-schedule) the six dead tests, close the two open [URGENT.md](URGENT.md) OTIS-weight follow-ups. ~hours of effort; prevents wasted days and lets the plan trust the TODO. |
| 22 | **OTIS CPU/GPU policy parity divergence + meaningless weights.** The native OTIS backend returns **raw policy-head logits**, skipping the per-legal-move refinement the CPU path applies ([Backend.java](src/chess/nn/otis/cuda/Backend.java):22-24, fact-check confirmed) ŌĆö so CUDA and CPU OTIS are NOT behaviorally identical at the policy level, only at WDL. Separately, the only shipped OTIS weights are a deterministic-random placeholder ([Model.java](src/chess/nn/otis/Model.java):32), and any pre-2026-06-02 weights are geometrically wrong (channel-10 pawn bug, [URGENT.md](URGENT.md)). | M | M | Fix the policy refinement in the native path so CPU==GPU at the policy level, and extend the parity test ([OtisBackendRegressionTest.java](src/testing/OtisBackendRegressionTest.java)) beyond WDL. Do NOT present OTIS numbers as meaningful until real weights are trained and re-exported post-fix. Until then, route reference-grade analysis through external UCI. |
| 23 | **Legal / fair-play concerns from import + analysis features.** B (import) and C (review) could be misread as cheating aids or run afoul of platform ToS / data terms; the ECO book and bundled weights carry separate upstream licenses (digest notes README flags this) and there is no SBOM/per-artifact license manifest in releases. | L | M | Keep features analysis/study-only, offline, post-game ŌĆö never live-game assistance (reinforces #1). Add a per-artifact license/provenance file to release bundles. State data terms for any imported source. The GPL-3.0-only license is clear for code; surface the *weights'* separate terms. |
| 24 | **Data privacy of a local game database.** A stores the user's own games (potentially identifying ŌĆö names, events, dates) in plaintext `dump/` JSONL. No encryption, no redaction, and exports may carry PII into datasets/manifests. | L | M | Keep all storage local (consistent with the boundary). Document that A's store is plaintext under the repo/`dump/` and not encrypted. For dataset exports, do not auto-stamp player names/event tags into provenance metadata unless explicitly requested. **ASSUMPTION:** no remote sync exists, so blast radius is local-disk only ŌĆö keep it that way. |
| 25 | **Overbuilding plugins / extension points.** L is explicitly a NON-GOAL ([TODO.txt](TODO.txt):632) yet the temptation recurs (pluggable explainers, custom exporters). A plugin framework fights determinism (third-party code in the pipeline), the no-deps build, and security for a single-maintainer project. | L | M | Reject L. The legitimate extension need ŌĆö adding a UCI engine ŌĆö is already met by config-as-extension via [Protocol.java](src/chess/uci/Protocol.java) TOML (a new engine is a config change, not code). Keep that seam healthy; build no general plugin loader. |
| 26 | **Trying to compete with online sites / Stockfish strength.** Re-litigating "make CRTK play stronger" or "add a web app" wastes effort against the boundary and against the in-house engine's explicit non-goal (`wiki/in-house-engine.md`: "It will not out-play Stockfish ... and it isn't trying to"). | L | H | Hold the line: in-house engine is for determinism/zero-deps; reference-grade strength routes to external UCI. No online surface. Make this explicit in the plan's "out of scope" section so it is not re-proposed each cycle. |
| 27 | **Research/visualization features crowd out core study workflows.** The TODO's heaviest themes (MCTS graph canvas, NN views, OTIS kernels, T5) are research/GUI niceties for users who already understand the internals; they do not help a student get their games into the tool. Continuing to fund them at P1 is mis-prioritization. | H | M | Sequence per the theme map: product foundations (F, A, C, I, M) at P0/P1; research/visualization polish demoted to P2/build-later. Keep only the *bug* inside the MCTS theme (live-NN start/end-only regression), not the net-new graph canvas. Cap Java-hygiene scans as continuous background, not a gate. |
| 28 | **PGN imports still need real-world corpus validation.** Focused mitigation now documents the FEN-without-SetUp compatibility policy, keeps explicit `SetUp=="0"` authoritative, consults `Variant` for Chess960 X-FEN normalization, pins parser/store fixtures, and runs a deterministic 2,048-game `PgnStoreScaleRegressionTest`. The remaining risk is whether messy real-world PGN corpora expose more malformed setup conventions. | M | M | Keep the focused SetUp/Chess960 fixtures and bounded scale regression as permanent gates; run broader opt-in real-world import trials before scaling A imports further. |

### Highest-leverage mitigations (synthesis)

Three mitigations retire the most risk and should be non-negotiable preconditions:

1. **Land F (schema + catalog + `schemaVersion`) before A/C/E/I extend any contract.** This single ordering retires #3, #4, #5, and the worst of #10. The metadata already exists in [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) ŌĆö generate, don't hand-author.
2. **Run M (roadmap reconciliation) first, in hours.** Retires #21 outright, surfaces #9/#19/#20/#22 as cheap fixes, and makes the rest of the plan trustworthy.
3. **Promote shared logic into `chess.*` core, never the GUI.** Keeps the one-shared-core and CLI-is-source-of-truth invariants intact, retiring #7 and bounding #6.

The risks that *cannot* be fully mitigated ŌĆö only contained ŌĆö are #2 (determinism under threading/wall-clock), #14 (FNV-as-key collisions at scale), and #16 (font-dependent PDF byte-stability). These should be stated as explicit, documented limitations rather than papered over with "byte-exact" claims the code does not actually guarantee.

---

## 21. Final recommendation

This section converts the theme verdicts, TODO reconciliation, and fact-check into a decision a single maintainer can act on this week. It is deliberately opinionated. Where the plan elsewhere lists 14 themes, this section says what to do *first* and what to refuse.

### The one-sentence thesis

CRTK is an exceptionally strong **chess-engine-and-data toolbox** that has no idea what to do with **your own games**. Every product gap that matters ŌĆö local game database (A), review-to-study routing (C), repertoire/SRS (D) ŌĆö is downstream of two cheap, foundational things that do not exist yet: a **machine-readable contract** (theme F) and an **honest, reconciled roadmap** (theme M). The merit of the codebase is real and verified; the roadmap pointing at it is stale and inward-facing.

---

### If you do only ONE thing

**Ship `crtk help --json` plus a `schemaVersion` field on the record format (theme F, the catalog slice).**

Why this one, decisively:

- It is the precondition for nearly everything else of value. The SDK/server (E), editor/notebook tooling (K), a stable on-disk game store (A), and study-unit output (C) all need a stable contract to build on. Today there is none ŌĆö verified: there are zero `*.schema.json` files in the repo, and no `crtk help --json`/`crtk schema` command in [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) (grep found neither). Agents and tools must scrape 69 KB of prose in [wiki/command-reference.md](wiki/command-reference.md).
- The metadata **already exists in memory**. `CliRegistry.buildRoot()` holds every area, action, alias, summary, usage, example, and `detailHelpKey` on [CliCommand](src/application/cli/CliCommand.java) nodes. Serializing the tree is hours, not weeks ŌĆö you are exposing data you already constructed, not inventing it.
- It is enforceable and self-consistent with the project's existing values. [WorkbenchCommandRegression](src/testing/WorkbenchCommandRegression.java) already walks `CliRegistry.root()` to prove the Workbench mirrors the CLI; a `help --json` regression that asserts the catalog covers every runnable leaf reuses that exact pattern.
- It pays off the project's own stated identity. The agent guide promises "[a program driving crtk should never have to guess](wiki/ai-agents.md)" ŌĆö yet there is no machine-readable catalog to make that true. This closes the single largest gap between claim and code in the docs.

If you ship nothing else, ship this.

---

### If you do only THREE things

In strict order. Each is small-to-medium, grounded, and unblocks the next.

#### 1. Reconcile the roadmap with HEAD (theme M ŌĆö small, P1, do first)

**Status 2026-06-16:** [x] Done for the stale `Threats.java` and repository
OTIS-weight follow-ups. `TODO.txt` now points at the existing Threats
implementation, and `URGENT.md` is resolved because the only default OTIS weight
is the randomized placeholder.

The TODO is actively dangerous to plan against. Verified stale claims:
- [TODO.txt](TODO.txt) calls `src/chess/tag/Threats.java` an "11-byte stub" with a ~25-line rebuild-from-spec block. The file is a real **10,600-byte** implementation wired into [Generator.java](src/chess/tag/Generator.java) at `addStructuralThreats` (line 920) and `tags()` (line 1097). A contributor following the TODO would rebuild finished code.
- The "OTIS CUDA Backend" theme is framed as "add a CUDA implementation," but `native/cuda/build/libotis_cuda.so` is already built, with [chess.nn.otis.cuda.Backend](src/chess/nn/otis/cuda/Backend.java) and passing parity tests. The real work there is one *correctness* fix (see below), not greenfield.
- [URGENT.md](URGENT.md) has two unresolved checkboxes (re-export pre-fix OTIS weights; delete the file). Close or convert to a tracked issue.

Cost: roughly an afternoon. Payoff: the team plans against reality, and the genuinely-absent themes (A/C/F) get named in the roadmap for the first time.

#### 2. Build theme F ŌĆö the schema/catalog foundation (medium, P0)

**Status 2026-06-16:** [x] Done for the foundation. The worktree now has
`crtk help --json`, `crtk schema list|show|validate`, `crtk record validate`,
`crtk.record.v2`, `crtk.record.training-jsonl.v1`,
`crtk.dataset.manifest.v1`, and agreement tests over real emitters.

The `help --json` catalog (the "one thing" above) **plus**:
- Add a `schemaVersion` field to [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) (verified absent today ŌĆö the format is a fixed 7-field shape with no version).
- Publish JSON Schema files for `.record`, `training-jsonl`, and the dataset `meta.json` shapes.
- Add a strict/fail-loud read path to [RecordIO.java](src/application/cli/RecordIO.java), since `Record.fromJson` and the readers currently drop malformed input silently ŌĆö corrosive to the "reproducible datasets" value.

#### 3. Land the foundation of theme A ŌĆö a local PGN store via `crtk pgn` (large, P1)

**Status 2026-06-16:** [x] Foundation landed. `chess.pgn.PgnStore` and
`crtk pgn import|show|find|stats|delete|compact` exist with append-safe JSONL,
side indexes, FEN-verified signature lookup, and focused compact/import/find
regressions. SetUp/Chess960 import hardening is covered by focused parser/store
regressions; bounded scale validation is covered by
`PgnStoreScaleRegressionTest` before scaling imports further.

This is where study/research value actually begins. The pieces exist but are in-memory and Workbench-only: [PgnExplorerModel.java](src/application/gui/workbench/game/PgnExplorerModel.java) does index/filter/dedupe with no CLI peer. Promote that logic into `chess.*` core and expose a noun-verb `crtk pgn import|index|query|show|stats` area over a JSONL/`.record`-backed store keyed on a game-id + `Position.signatureCore()`. This depends on F (it needs the versioned, game-id-carrying record schema), which is exactly why F comes first.

After these three, the path to C (review-to-study), G (deeper grounded explanations), and eventually D (SRS) is unobstructed. None of those should start before A and F exist.

---

### The NEXT PR (specific, small, grounded)

**Status 2026-06-16:** [x] Completed and expanded. The catalog shipped together
with schema discovery/validation and the record schemaVersion work that was
originally listed as out of scope. The Theme C engine-free classifier and
`crtk.review.ply.v1` row contract now exist; the next smallest PR should wire
the deterministic `crtk review game --offline` command before external-UCI
review modes.

**Title:** `Add crtk help --json machine-readable command catalog`

**Scope (one sitting, low risk):**
1. Add a `--json` branch to [HelpCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/HelpCommand.java) (or a new `schema` leaf) that walks `CliRegistry.root()` and emits one JSON object: areas ŌåÆ actions ŌåÆ `{ path, aliases, summary, usageTail, examples, runnable }`, plus the documented exit-code taxonomy (0/1/2/3 per [CommandFailure](src/application/cli/command/CommandFailure.java)).
2. Use the existing `utility.Json` serializer ŌĆö no hand-built `StringBuilder` JSON (the [EngineBatchCommand](src/application/cli/command/EngineBatchCommand.java) hand-assembly pattern is exactly what to avoid here).
3. Add a regression in [CLICommandRegressionTest.java](src/testing/CLICommandRegressionTest.java) asserting (a) the catalog round-trips through `utility.Json`, and (b) every runnable leaf in `CliRegistry.root()` appears ŌĆö mirroring the walk in [WorkbenchCommandRegression](src/testing/WorkbenchCommandRegression.java).

**Why this PR and not a bigger one:** it is additive (no behavior change to existing commands), it reuses metadata that already exists, it is testable with the in-house harness, and it is the literal precondition for E/K and a clean dependency for A/C. It also lets the next PR (record `schemaVersion`) reference a published contract instead of prose.

**Explicitly not in this PR:** no server, no SDK, no record schema change, no new dataset fields. Keep it to serialization + test.

---

### The NEXT README change (exact wording)

The current tagline in [README.md](README.md) is:

> **A deterministic chess programming toolkit.**

That is accurate but inward-facing ŌĆö it describes the *implementation property* (determinism) and the *audience* (programmers), not what a study/research user gets. Propose tightening it to name the data-and-study mission without overclaiming features that do not exist yet:

> **A deterministic, local-first toolkit for chess analysis, datasets, and publishing.**

Rationale, grounded:
- "local-first" is true and load-bearing ŌĆö it is the product boundary the whole plan defends (no online play/social/cloud).
- "analysis, datasets, and publishing" maps to three pillars that genuinely ship today: external-UCI analysis, `record dataset`/JSONL exports, and the native PDF book pipeline. It does **not** promise a game database or SRS, which are not built ŌĆö so the README stays honest.
- It keeps "deterministic," the project's strongest and most-verified property.

**Second, mandatory README/docs fix (a real bug, not a polish item):** [wiki/getting-started.md](wiki/getting-started.md) line 48 states "A prebuilt `crtk.jar` ships in the repository root," but `crtk.jar` is gitignored ([.gitignore](.gitignore) line 31). A fresh clone has no jar, so the documented `java -jar crtk.jar version` onboarding command fails. Fix the wording to instruct building first (`./scripts/run_regression_suite.sh jar` or `./install.sh`). This is a first-run footgun and should land in the same docs pass.

---

### What should NOT be worked on yet (and why)

Decisive refusals, consistent with the theme verdicts:

**Reject outright (do not build, now or as currently scoped):**
- **Plugins / extension points (L).** Already an explicit in-repo non-goal ([TODO.txt](TODO.txt) line 632: "NON-GOAL: a plugin framework"). Third-party code in the pipeline fights determinism, the no-deps build, and reproducibility. The legitimate need ŌĆö adding an engine ŌĆö is already met by config-as-extension via [Protocol.java](src/chess/uci/Protocol.java) TOML.
- **OTB / broadcast (N)** and **OCR/scan (O).** Both pull toward live/online or require a CV model the no-third-party-deps, plain-`javac` constraint cannot host. If recognition ever happens, it belongs in the external `chess-nn-playground` repo, and CRTK consumes its output as ordinary PGN via theme A. There is no in-boundary version worth starting.

**Defer (real merit, wrong time ŌĆö blocked on F/A):**
- **Local API server + SDKs (E).** Verified absent (no `ServerSocket`/`HttpServer` in src). Building it before F means hard-coding contracts F would replace. Acceptable later *only* as a localhost analysis/automation daemon ŌĆö never matchmaking/cloud.
- **VSCode/Jupyter tooling (K).** Parasitic on F (catalog) and ideally E (daemon, to avoid per-cell JVM startup). Today it would scrape prose ŌĆö the exact drift F kills.
- **Repertoire/SRS (D)** and **platform import/sync (B).** D is the capstone of the study loop and needs A+C+F+G first. B sits closest to the product boundary; the only acceptable slice is read-only PGN/file import, which folds into A's `pgn import` anyway.

**Demote within the existing (mostly-shipped) Workbench/research backlog ŌĆö keep, but not now:**
- The **Workbench MCTS graph canvas**, **NN-view polish**, **OTIS CUDA *kernel* optimization**, and **T5 model work** are internal research/GUI features. None moves the toolkit toward storing and studying a user's games. Specifically: optimizing OTIS throughput is premature because the only shipped OTIS weights are a deterministic-random placeholder ([Model.java](src/chess/nn/otis/Model.java), `otis_policy_wdl_random.bin`) ŌĆö you would be speeding up meaningless numbers. The T5 generative path is permanently stubbed ([T5PositionDescriptionGenerator](src/chess/describe/T5PositionDescriptionGenerator.java) `available()` is always false) and ships no weights, so it cannot deliver user value regardless of effort.
- **Java hygiene / SonarLint (TODO theme 1)** is fine as a *capped, continuous background stream*. Do not let "scan until zero warnings" gate any product work ŌĆö it is open-ended and user-invisible.

**Two cheap correctness items worth slotting in alongside the above (not standalone projects):**
- Fix the classifier default-weights drift: [Model.java](src/chess/nn/classifier/Model.java) line 17 points at `models/classifier_...bin` but the shipped file is `models/puzzle-classifier_...bin`, so `loadDefault()` is broken out of the box. One-line fix; bundle with the theme-I provenance pass.
- Close the OTIS CPU-vs-CUDA *policy* divergence: the native path returns raw policy-head logits and skips the per-legal-move refinement the Java path applies ([Backend.java](src/chess/nn/otis/cuda/Backend.java) lines 22ŌĆō24). This is the *one* OTIS-CUDA item worth keeping; it is correctness, not speed.

---

### The through-line

Stop polishing the toolbox; start letting users put their own games in it. The cheapest move that unlocks that ŌĆö and the one this plan keeps returning to ŌĆö is making the toolbox **describe itself in JSON** (F) and **tell the truth about what it already is** (M). Do those two first, in that PR-sized order, and every harder theme gets dramatically cheaper.

---

## 22. Engineering tooling & supporting software

The sections above describe *product* surfaces. This section describes the *engineering aids* an implementer (an AI coding agent + the maintainer) must build or extend to land those surfaces observably and safely. The plan front-loads **Theme F** (machine-readable catalog ŌåÆ JSON Schemas ŌåÆ fail-loud validation) and the **M0** reconciliation/correctness fixes precisely because almost everything downstream ŌĆö the serve daemon, SDKs, the PGN store, the review router, dataset provenance ŌĆö silently drifts or hard-codes contracts unless those land first. The single highest-leverage tool is the `crtk help --json` catalog generator: it is the contract source the rest of the toolchain builds against, and ┬¦21 already names it the "if you do one thing" deliverable.

Every tool below honors the same hard constraints as the product code: plain `javac --release 17`, **zero third-party Java dependencies**, the in-house test harness (`testing.TestSupport`, public-static-`main`, **not** JUnit, wired through [run_regression_suite.sh](scripts/run_regression_suite.sh)), CLI-mirrors-GUI, and deterministic golden output. A proposed tool that breaks one of these is wrong by construction. JSON is emitted only through [utility.Json](src/utility/Json.java); TOML only through [utility.Toml](src/utility/Toml.java); SHA-256 only through the existing [RunManifest](src/application/gui/workbench/session/RunManifest.java)`.sha256(Path)` helper (line 427) lifted into a shared `chess.io` location.

### 22.1 Build these first (the unblock shortlist)

| # | Status | Tool | Build / Extend | Milestone ŌåÆ what it unblocks |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | [x] | **`crtk help --json` catalog generator** + `CommandCatalogRegressionTest` | extend [CliRegistry.java](src/application/cli/CliRegistry.java) / [HelpCommand.java](src/application/cli/command/HelpCommand.java) | **M1-1 / F** ŌĆö the contract E, K, A, C and the GUI mirror all build against; retires the "4th source of drift" risk |
| 2 | [x] | **`chess.schema` subset validator** + `schemas/*.schema.json` (record.v2 first) + `SchemaAgreementRegressionTest` | build-new `src/chess/schema/` | **M1-3 / F** ŌĆö makes contracts validatable; the witness test that catches "code added a field, schema didn't" |
| 3 | [x] | **`record validate` / `--strict` fail-loud ingestion** | extend [RecordIO](src/application/cli/RecordIO.java) / keep `Record.fromJson` tolerant for compatibility | **M1-4 / F** ŌĆö stops silent dataset shrink, the headline reproducibility precondition |
| 4 | [x] | **Regression-suite wiring** + resurrect 2 orphaned ML tests + non-JDK import-ban + per-step CI timeouts | extend [run_regression_suite.sh](scripts/run_regression_suite.sh) + `SourceHeaderRegressionTest` | **M0-4 / F** ŌĆö makes every new golden actually gate CI; holds the zero-deps line |
| 5 | [x] | **Byte-equality determinism harness** (`DatasetDeterminismRegressionTest`) | build-new | **M8-2 / I** ŌĆö makes the "byte-exact" claim testable |
| 6 | [x] | **Shared `chess.io.DatasetManifest` + `Provenance` helper** | extend ŌĆö route JSON via `utility.Json` | **M8-1 / I** ŌĆö one manifest across every exporter; no 3rd SHA-256 copy |
| 7 | [x] | **`chess.pgn` core store + FEN-verified signature index** | build-new `src/chess/pgn/` | **M2-1 / A** ŌĆö the keystone study-foundation gap, in core not GUI |

### 22.2 Tooling catalog

**A. Schema & contract tooling (Theme F ŌĆö front-loaded).**

| Tool | Build/Extend | Pri | Purpose (one line) |
|---|---|---|---|
| `crtk help --json` catalog generator | extend `CliRegistry`/`HelpCommand` | P0 | Serialize the in-memory `CliCommand` tree to one versioned, deterministic catalog (`crtk.cli.catalog.v1`) ŌĆö generated, never hand-authored |
| `chess.schema` subset validator | build-new `src/chess/schema/` | P0 | From-scratch interpreter over a pragmatic JSON-Schema subset (type/required/properties/items/enum/const/local `$ref`) built only on `utility.Json`; rejects unsupported keywords loudly |
| Published `schemas/*.schema.json` (~20) | build-new files + add `schemaVersion` to [Record.java](src/chess/struct/Record.java) | P1 | record.v2, training-jsonl, analysis-delta, dataset-manifest + provisional v1 for review-row/study-task/repertoire-card/db/import manifests, each derived from the real emitter |
| `SchemaAgreementRegressionTest` + `crtk schema check` gate | build-new, wired into CI | P0 | Capture golden bytes from the real Java emitter, assert they validate against the schema file ŌĆö the schema becomes a second independent witness |
| `crtk record validate` / `--strict` | extend `RecordIO`/`Record.fromJson` | P0 | First invalid object ŌåÆ per-line `{index,line,field,message}` on stderr + non-zero exit (reuse code 3); default stays tolerant for back-compat |
| `crtk schema list` / `show` | extend `CliRegistry` | P2 | Lets agents/editors fetch schemas (jar resources) without filesystem knowledge |

**B. Test / golden / regression / determinism harnesses.**

| Tool | Build/Extend | Pri | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|
| `DatasetDeterminismRegressionTest` | build-new | P0 | Run each exporter twice on fixed input; assert byte-identical tensors + manifest hashes after stripping the explicitly-listed time fields |
| Golden-fixture corpus for new artifacts | extend `testdata/` | P1 | A fixed game ŌåÆ `review-row.v1` ŌåÆ `study-task.v1` committed golden + a golden `--analyze-game` once the dynamic tag families are registered |
| Regression-suite wiring + orphan resurrection + import-ban | extend `run_regression_suite.sh` + `SourceHeaderRegressionTest` | P0 | Wire `RecordTrainingJSONLRegressionTest` + `RecordLC0ExporterRegressionTest` (exist but unreferenced ŌåÆ pass by not running); ban `import org.*`/`com.*` non-JDK and `chess.*`ŌåÆ`application.*` |
| `ServeRegressionTest` (one-impl equivalence) | build-new | P1 | Start the daemon on an ephemeral loopback port; diff `/run` stdout byte-for-byte (time-stripped) against `TestSupport.runMain` of identical argv; assert exit-code taxonomy and budget clamp-never-raises |
| `ReviewRouterRegressionTest` (engine-pinned) | extend UCI-test convention | P1 | Pin engine binary + protocol TOML + `--threads 1` + explicit budgets; assert a known blunder ŌåÆ `quality=blunder` at the right ply; reuse `fake-uci.sh` so CI needs no real Stockfish |
| [x] `ReviewClassifierRegressionTest` (pure-function) | build-new | P0 | Pins `chess.review.Classifier`, WDL blunder gating, severity inputs, and the only-move / already-decided / dead-draw / theory / blitz false-positive guards as engine-free goldens |
| [x] `ReviewRowSchemaRegressionTest` (schema/golden) | build-new | P0 | Pins `chess.review.ReviewRow`, `crtk.review.ply.v1`, byte-stable JSON emission, tag-delta shape, and the reproducibility block before review command orchestration |
| [x] `ReviewCommandRegressionTest` (offline + UCI CLI) | build-new | P0 | Pins `crtk review game --offline`, bounded fake-UCI review, PGN mainline parsing, schema-valid review JSONL, deterministic offline repro metadata, external protocol/budget metadata, grounded dynamic tags, and usage failure for missing PGN input |
| `RepertoireRegressionTest` (state-transition) | build-new | P1 | SM-2 golden **integers** (no float, no wall clock), hard overload caps, transposition collapse, illegal-import-fails-loud, PGN round-trip identity ŌĆö the one mutable schema that can't use byte-golden |
| `ExplainRegressionTest` (verifier-rejection) | build-new | P1 | Assert the verifier rejects each ungrounded class and that classical prose is always `grounded==true` over a Chess960/mate/stalemate fixture set ŌĆö never pins exact wording |
| End-to-end review-pipeline golden harness | build-new | P1 | Diff every intermediate artifact (importŌåÆŌĆ”ŌåÆrun-manifest) byte-for-byte on a small committed PGN; the only way to *see* the multi-stage glue holds |
| [x] Multi-source PGN round-trip + SetUp/Chess960 corpus | build-new fixtures | P1 | Covered by focused parser/store fixtures for SetUp/FEN precedence and Variant-tagged Chess960 X-FEN normalization |
| [x] Bounded larger-corpus PGN-store benchmark | build-new `PgnStoreScaleRegressionTest` | P1 | Imports a deterministic 2,048-game corpus through the real file path and gates sidecar counts, reopen behavior, representative FEN lookups, and duplicate-idempotent import |

**C. Data / provenance / dataset tools (Theme I).**

| Tool | Build/Extend | Pri | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|
| `chess.io.DatasetManifest` + `Provenance` helper | extend (reuse `RunManifest.sha256`) | P1 | One `crtk.dataset.manifest.v1` from every exporter: version, git commit, argv, per-input/output/weights/engine SHA-256, label/dedupe/split policy, Filter-DSL hashes, row counts |
| `crtk dataset verify` / `audit` + `dataset diff` | build-new `DatasetCommand` verbs | P1 | Re-hash outputs vs manifest, exit non-zero naming the drifted file; `diff` explains *why* two exports differ (input hash vs filter vs version vs weights) |
| `record split` / `dedupe` / `audit-split` | build-new over `RecordIO` streaming | P1 | Group-aware deterministic split (`hash(seedŌĆ¢group_key)`, never input order/clock) so transpositions can't straddle splits; `audit-split` proves no leakage |
| `--row-hashes` sidecar (`.rowhashes.txt`) | extend exporters | P2 | done with `sha256(raw-record-json-v1)` per emitted logical row; semantic FEN+label hashes remain a future algorithm |
| `analyzed.jsonl ŌåÆ Record` adapter | build-new | P1 | Bridges the seam where `analyze-batch` emits hand-built JSONL but `analysis-delta` consumes `Record.analysis`; preserves parent/child lineage |
| `tools/crtk_dataset.py` + `jsonl_to_parquet.py` | build-new under `tools/` | P2 | ~50-line numpy+json helpers; Parquet/HF stays a documented pandas recipe (user-installed), never a Java dep |

**D. PGN store & review/repertoire data tools (Themes A / C / D).**

| Tool | Build/Extend | Pri | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|
| `chess.pgn` core store + FEN-verified signature index | build-new `src/chess/pgn/` | P1 | Append-safe JSONL store + `gameIdŌåÆ(shard,offset)` sidecar + per-position `signatureCore()` index; store full FEN beside the FNV signature and verify on FEN equality at lookup; single-writer |
| `crtk db import/find/show/stats/sources/dedupe/compact` + ingest report | build-new `DbCommand` + `DbStoreRegressionTest` | P1 | Idempotent import keyed on `gameId`+`signatureCore`; `db show --format pgn` byte-equals `Pgn.toPgn`; `{file,games_parsed,imported,duplicates,malformed}` JSONL report is the agent-consumable surface |
| Platform `GameSource` adapters (Folder/Lichess/Chess.com) + fixture HTTP server | build-new `chess.platform` | P1 | Fetch-only via JDK `java.net.http` (no dep), kept out of `chess.core`; resumable + `--cache` replays offline; token env-only with a leak-scanner regression; tested against a hermetic `com.sun.net.httpserver` fixture |
| Engine-graded verdict pipeline + study-unit emitter | extend `Engine`/`MineCommand`/`RecordAnalysisDeltaCommand` | P1 | Route per-move deltas through external UCI, attach graded verdicts to MOVE_EFFECT, emit a published-schema puzzle Record per turning point (the "human played X, study the refutation" pipeline) |
| `chess.repertoire` core + `RepertoireCommand` | build-new `chess.repertoire` | P1 | Integer-only SM-2 scheduler (no floats/clock), deterministic time-budgeted planner with 3 hard caps, PGN round-trip (no lock-in), weights fail-soft to uniform when the store is absent |
| Tag-family registration in `Sort.FAMILY_ORDER` + `Literals` | extend [Sort.java](src/chess/tag/Sort.java) + `chess.tag.core.Literals` | P1 | Register MOVE_EFFECT/LINE/VARIATION/GAME (confirmed **absent** at Sort.java:24) so dynamic families route through canonical sort/dedupe/Filter ŌĆö M0 prerequisite for C |
